UPDATE LOANTRANSACTION A SET 
(CATEGORYCODE, GRADECODE)=
(
    SELECT CATEGORYCODE, GRADECODE FROM PISEMPLOYEEMASTER
    WHERE COMPANYCODE=A.COMPANYCODE
    AND DIVISIONCODE=A.DIVISIONCODE
    AND A.TOKENNO=A.TOKENNO
    AND A.WORKERSERIAL=A.WORKERSERIAL
)


SELECT * FROM MENUMASTER_RND
WHERE UPPER(MENUDESC) LIKE UPPER('%loan entry%')

--MODIFY VW_WPSPISMASTER VIEW

DROP VIEW BIRLANEW.VW_WPSPISMASTER;

/* Formatted on 03/08/2020 7:22:42 PM (QP5 v5.115.810.9015) */
CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE VIEW BIRLANEW.VW_WPSPISMASTER
(
   WORKERTYPE,
   COMPANYCODE,
   DIVISIONCODE,
   WORKERSERIAL,
   WORKERCODE,
   WORKERNAME,
   FATHERNAME,
   DEPARTMENTCODE,
   DEPARTMENTNAME,
   CATEGORYCODE,
   CATEGORYNAME,
   GRADECODE,
   GRADEDESC,
   DATEOFBIRTH,
   DATEOFJOINING,
   ESIJOININGDATE,
   PFJOINIGDATE,
   ESINO,
   PFNO,
   PENSIONNO,
   DATEOFRETIREMENT,
   EMPLOYEEMARRIED,
   SEX,
   SPOUSENAME,
   EMPLOYEESTATUS,
   STATUSDATE,
   FORM3CEASEDATE,
   PFSETTELMENTDATE,
   ADDRESS,
   INACTIVE,
   FORM3RECEIPTDATE,
   PFCATEGORY,
   ADHARCARDNO,
   UANNO,
   BANKACNO,
   BANKCODE,
   BANKACCHOLDINGNAME
)
AS
--   SELECT   'WPS' WORKERTYPE,
--            A.COMPANYCODE,
--            A.DIVISIONCODE,
--            A.WORKERSERIAL,
--            A.TOKENNO AS WORKERCODE,
--            A.WORKERNAME,
--            A.FATHERNAME,
--            A.DEPARTMENTCODE,
--            D.DEPARTMENTNAME,
--            A.WORKERCATEGORYCODE AS CATEGORYCODE,
--            B.WORKERCATEGORYNAME AS CATEGORYNAME,
--            GRADECODE,
--            ' ' GRADEDESC,
--            A.DATEOFBIRTH DATEOFBIRTH,
--            A.DATEOFJOINING,
--            A.ESIJOININGDATE,
--            A.PFMEMBERSHIPDATE AS PFJOINIGDATE,
--            A.ESINO,
--            A.PFNO,
--            A.PENSIONNO,
--            A.DATEOFRETIREMENT,
--            CASE WHEN A.MARITALSTATUS = 'M' THEN 'Y' ELSE 'N' END
--               EMPLOYEEMARRIED,
--            A.SEX,
--            A.WORKERSOUSENAME SPOUSENAME,
--            WORKERSTATUS EMPLOYEESTATUS,
--            DATEOFTERMINATION STATUSDATE,
--            DATEOFTERMINATIONADVICE FORM3CEASEDATE,
--            PFSETTELMENTDATE,
--            ADDRESS1 || ADDRESS2 || ADDRESS3 || ADDRESS4 || ADDRESS5 ADDRESS,
--            CASE
--               WHEN PFSETTELMENTDATE IS NULL
--                    AND NVL (TAKEPARTINWAGES, 'N') = 'N'
--               THEN
--                  'Y'
--               ELSE
--                  'N'
--            END
--               INACTIVE,
--            DATEOFTERMINATIONADVICE AS FORM3RECEIPTDATE,
--            PFCATEGORY AS PFCATEGORY,
--            A.ADHARCARDNO,
--            A.UANNO,
--            A.BANKACNO,
--            A.BANKCODE,
--            A.WORKERNAME_BANK BANKACCHOLDINGNAME
--     FROM   WPSWORKERMAST A, WPSWORKERCATEGORYMAST B, DEPARTMENTMASTER D
--    WHERE       A.DivisionCode = B.DivisionCode
--            AND A.WORKERCATEGORYCODE = B.WORKERCATEGORYCODE
--            AND A.DivisionCode = D.DivisionCode
--            AND A.DEPARTMENTCODE = D.DEPARTMENTCODE
--   UNION ALL
   SELECT   'PIS' WORKERTYPE,
            A.COMPANYCODE,
            A.DIVISIONCODE,
            A.WORKERSERIAL,
            A.TOKENNO AS WORKERCODE,
            A.EMPLOYEENAME AS WORKERNAME,
            A.FATHERNAME FATHERNAME,
            A.DEPARTMENTCODE,
            D.DEPARTMENTDESC,
            A.CATEGORYCODE AS CATEGORYCODE,
            B.CATEGORYDESC AS CATEGORYNAME,
            A.GRADECODE,
            C.GRADEDESC AS GRADEDESC,
            A.DATEOFBIRTH DATEOFBIRTH,
            A.DATEOFJOIN AS DATEOFJOINING,
            NULL AS ESIJOININGDATE,
            A.PFENTITLEDATE AS PFJOINIGDATE,
            A.ESINO,
            A.PFNO,
            TO_CHAR (A.PENSIONNO) PENSIONNO,
            CASE
               WHEN A.EXTENDEDRETIREDATE IS NULL THEN A.DATEOFRETIRE
               ELSE A.EXTENDEDRETIREDATE
            END
               DATEOFRETIREMENT,
            A.MARITIALSTATUS AS MARRIED,
            A.SEX,
            A.SPOUSENAME SPOUSENAME,
            A.EMPLOYEESTATUS,
            A.STATUSDATE,
            A.STATUSDATE FORM3CEASEDATE,
            PFSETTELMENTDATE,
            A.ADDRESS_PERMANENT ADDRESS,
            CASE
               WHEN A.PFSETTELMENTDATE IS NULL
                    AND A.EMPLOYEESTATUS <> 'ACTIVE'
               THEN
                  'Y'
               ELSE
                  'N'
            END
               INACTIVE,
            STATUSDATE AS FORM3RECEIPTDATE,
            'N' AS PFCATEGORY,
            A.AADHARNO,
            A.UANNO,
            A.BANKACCNUMBER BANKACNO,
            A.BANKCODE,
            A.BANKACCHOLDINGNAME
     FROM   PISEMPLOYEEMASTER A,
            PISCATEGORYMASTER B,
            PISGRADEMASTER C,
            PISDEPARTMENTMASTER D
    WHERE       A.DIVISIONCODE = B.DIVISIONCODE
            AND A.CATEGORYCODE = B.CATEGORYCODE
            AND A.DIVISIONCODE = C.DIVISIONCODE
            AND A.CATEGORYCODE = C.CATEGORYCODE
            AND A.GRADECODE = C.GRADECODE
            AND A.DIVISIONCODE = D.DIVISIONCODE
            AND A.DEPARTMENTCODE = D.DEPARTMENTCODE;

--INSERT TO SYS_AUTOGEN_PARAMS FOR LOANTRANSACTION 
Insert into SYS_AUTOGEN_PARAMS
   (COMPANYCODE, DIVISIONCODE, YEARCODE, PARAM_NAME, TOT_LENGTH, 
    PREFIX, SUFFIX, ACT_TABLENAME, ACT_COL_NAME, PADDING_LENGTH, 
    SEQUENCER_NAME, PURPOSE)
 Values
   ('BJ0056', '0001', '2020-2021', 'LOAN TRANSACTION', 16, 
    'LNTRN/<<Y1Y2>>/', NULL, 'LOANTRANSACTION', 'APPLICATIONNO', 5, 
    NULL, NULL);
COMMIT;

PROC_SD_GTTVSACTUAL_SYNC




SELECT * FROM SYS_TFMAP
WHERE SYS_TABLENAME_ACTUAL='LOANTRANSACTION'


EXEC PROC_CREATE_GBL_TMP_TABLES(5027,0)

SELECT * FROM LOANTRANSACTION WHERE TOKENNO IN ('00920','00958')

SELECT * FROM SYS_HELP_QRY
WHERE QRY_ID = '6100'

--ADD  HELP QRY WITH ID 6100
Insert into SYS_HELP_QRY
   (QRY_ID, QRY_STRING, PARAMETER_STRING, QRY_SHORTDESC, QRY_RETURN_TABLE_NAME, 
    WEB_QRY_STRING, SEARCH_COLUMNLIST, MODULENAME)
 Values
   (6100, '""', 'COMPANYCODE~DIVISIONCODE~WORKERSERIAL~PATTERN', 'LOAN INFROMATION', NULL, 
    'SELECT APPLICATIONNO,L.TOKENNO,WORKERNAME EMPLOYEENAME,LOANCODE,TO_CHAR(LOANDATE,''DD/MM/YYYY'') LOANDATE, L.MODULE'||CHR(13)||CHR(10)||'FROM LOANTRANSACTION L, VW_WPSPISMASTER /* PISEMPLOYEEMASTER*/  E'||CHR(13)||CHR(10)||'WHERE L.COMPANYCODE=E.COMPANYCODE'||CHR(13)||CHR(10)||'      AND L.DIVISIONCODE=E.DIVISIONCODE'||CHR(13)||CHR(10)||'      AND L.WORKERSERIAL=E.WORKERSERIAL'||CHR(13)||CHR(10)||'      AND L.COMPANYCODE=<<COMPANYCODE>>  '||CHR(13)||CHR(10)||'      AND L.DIVISIONCODE=<<DIVISIONCODE>>'||CHR(13)||CHR(10)||'      AND L.WORKERSERIAL=<<WORKERSERIAL>>'||CHR(13)||CHR(10)||'      AND L.LOANCODE = <<LOANCODE>>'||CHR(13)||CHR(10)||'ORDER BY L.LOANDATE DESC', 'TOKENNO~EMPLOYEENAME~', 'PIS');
COMMIT;


SELECT APPLICATIONNO,L.TOKENNO,WORKERNAME EMPLOYEENAME,LOANCODE,TO_CHAR(LOANDATE,'DD/MM/YYYY') LOANDATE, L.MODULE
FROM LOANTRANSACTION L, VW_WPSPISMASTER /* PISEMPLOYEEMASTER*/  E
WHERE L.COMPANYCODE=E.COMPANYCODE
      AND L.DIVISIONCODE=E.DIVISIONCODE
      AND L.WORKERSERIAL=E.WORKERSERIAL
      AND L.COMPANYCODE=<<COMPANYCODE>>  
      AND L.DIVISIONCODE=<<DIVISIONCODE>>
      AND L.WORKERSERIAL=<<WORKERSERIAL>>
      AND L.LOANCODE = <<LOANCODE>>
ORDER BY L.LOANDATE DESC

DESC VW_WPSPISMASTER

DELETE FROM GBL_PISLEAVEBALANCE;
    
SELECT * FROM GBL_PISLEAVEBALANCE
WHERE TOKENNO='0049'

exec PRC_PIS_LEAVEBALANCE ('0001','003','2020-2021','202004','')
 

select * from (
   select times_purchased, state_code
   from customers t
)
pivot 
(
   count(state_code)
   for state_code in ('NY','CT','NJ','FL','MO')
)
order by times_purchased

SELECT * FROM (

SELECT A.TOKENNO,B.YEARCODE,CALENDARYEAR,A.YEARMONTH,A.LEAVECODE,A.LV_TAKEN,A.LV_BAL,ENTITLEMENTS,CARRYFORWARD FROM
(
    SELECT * FROM GBL_PISLEAVEBALANCE
) A,
(   
    SELECT * FROM  PISLEAVEENTITLEMENT
    WHERE YEARCODE='2019-2020'
) B
WHERE A.COMPANYCODE=B.COMPANYCODE
AND A.DIVISIONCODE=B.DIVISIONCODE
AND A.LEAVECODE	= B.LEAVECODE	
AND A.TOKENNO=B.TOKENNO

)
pivot 
(
   MAX(LV_BAL)
   for LEAVECODE in ('PL' AS PL,'SL' AS SL)
)


select value
from
(
    (
        select
            'a' v1,
            'e' v2,
            'i' v3,
            'o' v4,
            'u' v5
        from dual
    )
    unpivot
    (
        value
        for value_type in
            (v1,v2,v3,v4,v5)
    )
)
/

SELECT * FROM 
(   
    SELECT *  FROM 
    (
        SELECT A.COMPANYCODE, A.DIVISIONCODE,A.TOKENNO,B.YEARCODE,CALENDARYEAR,A.YEARMONTH,A.LEAVECODE,A.LV_TAKEN AVL,A.LV_BAL BAL,ENTITLEMENTS ERN FROM
        (
            SELECT * FROM GBL_PISLEAVEBALANCE
        ) A,
        (   
            SELECT * FROM  PISLEAVEENTITLEMENT
            WHERE YEARCODE='2019-2020'
        ) B
        WHERE A.COMPANYCODE=B.COMPANYCODE
        AND A.DIVISIONCODE=B.DIVISIONCODE
        AND A.LEAVECODE	= B.LEAVECODE	
        AND A.TOKENNO=B.TOKENNO
    )
    UNPIVOT 
    (
       VALUE
       FOR COMPONENTNAME IN (AVL,BAL,ERN)
    )
)
PIVOT 
(
   MAX(VALUE)
   FOR LEAVECODE IN ('PL' AS PL,'SL' AS SL)
)




---------------------------------------------------------


SELECT COMPANYCODE, DIVISIONCODE, YEARMONTH, UNITCODE, DEPARTMENTCODE, CATEGORYCODE, GRADECODE,
WORKERSERIAL, TOKENNO,COMPONENTCODE,COMPONENTVALUE,
DECODE(COMPONENTCODE,'YTD_PF','Y.T.D. PF','YTD_FPF','Y.T.D. FP','YTD_VPF','Y.T.D. VPF','YTD_EC','Y.T.D. EC','YTD_GR','Y.T.D. GR','PFLN_BAL','PFLN BAL','SADV_BAL','SADV BAL','FEST_BAL','FEST BAL','PENSION','PENSION','PF_COMP','PF COMP') COMPONENTSHORTNAME,
1 PHASE, 
DECODE(COMPONENTCODE,'YTD_PF',1,'YTD_FPF',2,'YTD_VPF',3,'YTD_EC',4,'YTD_GR',5,'PFLN_BAL',6,'SADV_BAL',7,'FEST_BAL',8,'PENSION',9,'PF_COMP',10) CALCULATIONINDEX,COMPONENTTYPE FROM 
(
    SELECT A.COMPANYCODE,A.DIVISIONCODE, A.TOKENNO,'202004' YEARMONTH, A.UNITCODE, A.DEPARTMENTCODE, A.CATEGORYCODE, A.GRADECODE, A.WORKERSERIAL,'YTD' COMPONENTTYPE,
    SUM(NVL(PF_E,0)) YTD_PF,SUM(NVL(FPF,0)) YTD_FPF ,0 YTD_VPF ,0 YTD_EC ,0 YTD_GR ,0 PFLN_BAL ,0 SADV_BAL ,0 FEST_BAL ,0 PENSION ,0 PF_COMP 
    FROM PISPAYTRANSACTION A
    WHERE COMPANYCODE='0001'
    AND DIVISIONCODE='001' AND WORKERSERIAL IN  ( SELECT DISTINCT WORKERSERIAL FROM GTT_PISPAYSLIP_ED )
    AND TO_NUMBER(YEARMONTH) >= TO_NUMBER('202004')
    AND TO_NUMBER(YEARMONTH) <= TO_NUMBER('202004')
    GROUP BY A.COMPANYCODE,A.DIVISIONCODE, A.TOKENNO,A.UNITCODE, A.DEPARTMENTCODE, A.CATEGORYCODE, A.GRADECODE, A.WORKERSERIAL
)
UNPIVOT
(
    COMPONENTVALUE
    FOR COMPONENTCODE IN (YTD_PF,YTD_FPF,YTD_VPF,YTD_EC,YTD_GR,PFLN_BAL,SADV_BAL,FEST_BAL,PENSION,PF_COMP)
)



INSERT INTO GTT_PISPAYSLIP_ED_BIRLA
(
    COMPANYCODE, DIVISIONCODE, YEARMONTH, UNITCODE, DEPARTMENTCODE, CATEGORYCODE, GRADECODE, 
    WORKERSERIAL, TOKENNO, COMPONENTCODE,COMPONENTVALUE, COMPONENTSHORTNAME, PHASE, CALCULATIONINDEX, COMPONENTTYPE
)
SELECT COMPANYCODE, DIVISIONCODE, YEARMONTH, UNITCODE, DEPARTMENTCODE, CATEGORYCODE, GRADECODE,
WORKERSERIAL, TOKENNO,LEAVECODE COMPONENTCODE,COMPONENTVALUE,
DECODE(COMPONENTCODE,'AVL','AVL','BAL','BAL','ERN','ERN') COMPONENTSHORTNAME,
1 PHASE, 
DECODE(COMPONENTCODE,'ERN',1,'AVL',2,'BAL',3) CALCULATIONINDEX,'LEAVE' COMPONENTTYPE FROM 
(
    SELECT A.COMPANYCODE, A.DIVISIONCODE,A.YEARMONTH,B.YEARCODE,B.UNITCODE,null DEPARTMENTCODE,B.CATEGORYCODE, B.GRADECODE,
    A.WORKERSERIAL,A.TOKENNO,A.LEAVECODE,A.LV_TAKEN AVL,A.LV_BAL BAL,ENTITLEMENTS ERN FROM
    (
    SELECT * FROM GBL_PISLEAVEBALANCE
    ) A,
    (   
    SELECT * FROM  PISLEAVEENTITLEMENT
    WHERE YEARCODE='2019-2020'
    ) B
    WHERE A.COMPANYCODE=B.COMPANYCODE
    AND A.DIVISIONCODE=B.DIVISIONCODE
    AND A.LEAVECODE	= B.LEAVECODE	
    AND A.TOKENNO=B.TOKENNO
    AND A.TOKENNO='0049'
)
UNPIVOT
(
    COMPONENTVALUE
    FOR COMPONENTCODE IN (AVL,BAL,ERN)
)



SELECT * FROM GTT_PISPAYSLIP_ED_BIRLA
--WHERE COMPONENTTYPE='LEAVE'
WHERE TOKENNO='0049'

DELETE FROM GTT_PISPAYSLIP_ED_BIRLA
--WHERE COMPONENTTYPE='LEAVE'
WHERE TOKENNO<>'0049'

--ASSIGN 1

BASIC RT:           BASIC_RT
FIX/V.D.A  RT:
OT. HRS:

SELECT * FROM PISPAYTRANSACTION


INSERT INTO GTT_PISPAYSLIP_ED_BIRLA
(
    COMPANYCODE, DIVISIONCODE, YEARMONTH, UNITCODE, DEPARTMENTCODE, CATEGORYCODE, GRADECODE, 
    WORKERSERIAL, TOKENNO, COMPONENTCODE,COMPONENTVALUE, COMPONENTSHORTNAME, PHASE, CALCULATIONINDEX, COMPONENTTYPE
)
SELECT COMPANYCODE, DIVISIONCODE, YEARMONTH, UNITCODE, DEPARTMENTCODE, CATEGORYCODE, GRADECODE,
WORKERSERIAL, TOKENNO,COMPONENTCODE,COMPONENTVALUE,
DECODE(COMPONENTCODE,'BASIC_RT','BASIC RT','FIX_VDA_RT','FIX/V.D.A  RT','OT_HRS','OT. HRS') COMPONENTSHORTNAME,
1 PHASE, 
DECODE(COMPONENTCODE,'BASIC_RT',1,'FIX_VDA_RT',2,'OT_HRS',3) CALCULATIONINDEX,COMPONENTTYPE FROM 
(
    SELECT A.COMPANYCODE,A.DIVISIONCODE, A.TOKENNO,'202004' YEARMONTH, A.UNITCODE, A.DEPARTMENTCODE, A.CATEGORYCODE, A.GRADECODE, A.WORKERSERIAL,'ASSIGN1' COMPONENTTYPE,
    SUM(NVL(BASIC_RT,0)) BASIC_RT,0 FIX_VDA_RT ,0 OT_HRS 
    FROM PISPAYTRANSACTION A
    WHERE COMPANYCODE='0001'
    AND DIVISIONCODE='003' AND WORKERSERIAL IN  ( SELECT DISTINCT WORKERSERIAL FROM GTT_PISPAYSLIP_ED_BIRLA )
    AND TO_NUMBER(YEARMONTH) >= TO_NUMBER('202004')
    AND TO_NUMBER(YEARMONTH) <= TO_NUMBER('202004')
    GROUP BY A.COMPANYCODE,A.DIVISIONCODE, A.TOKENNO,A.UNITCODE, A.DEPARTMENTCODE, A.CATEGORYCODE, A.GRADECODE, A.WORKERSERIAL
)
UNPIVOT
(
    COMPONENTVALUE
    FOR COMPONENTCODE IN (BASIC_RT,FIX_VDA_RT,OT_HRS)
)


---------------------------------------------------------------
--ASSIGN 2

SPL/TRNG ALLW:
PERS. PAY RT:
OT. RT.:


SELECT * FROM PISPAYTRANSACTION


INSERT INTO GTT_PISPAYSLIP_ED_BIRLA
(
    COMPANYCODE, DIVISIONCODE, YEARMONTH, UNITCODE, DEPARTMENTCODE, CATEGORYCODE, GRADECODE, 
    WORKERSERIAL, TOKENNO, COMPONENTCODE,COMPONENTVALUE, COMPONENTSHORTNAME, PHASE, CALCULATIONINDEX, COMPONENTTYPE
)

SELECT COMPANYCODE, DIVISIONCODE, YEARMONTH, UNITCODE, DEPARTMENTCODE, CATEGORYCODE, GRADECODE,
WORKERSERIAL, TOKENNO,COMPONENTCODE,COMPONENTVALUE,
DECODE(COMPONENTCODE,'SPL_ALLW','SPL/TRNG ALLW','PERS_ALLW','PERS. PAY RT','OT_RT','OT. RT.') COMPONENTSHORTNAME,
1 PHASE, 
DECODE(COMPONENTCODE,'SPL_ALLW',1,'PERS_ALLW',2,'OT_RT',3) CALCULATIONINDEX,COMPONENTTYPE FROM 
(
    SELECT A.COMPANYCODE,A.DIVISIONCODE, A.TOKENNO,'202004' YEARMONTH, A.UNITCODE, A.DEPARTMENTCODE, A.CATEGORYCODE, A.GRADECODE, A.WORKERSERIAL,
    'ASSIGN2' COMPONENTTYPE,
    0 SPL_ALLW, SUM(A.PERS_ALLW) PERS_ALLW,0 OT_RT
    FROM PISPAYTRANSACTION A
    WHERE COMPANYCODE='0001'
    AND DIVISIONCODE='003' AND WORKERSERIAL IN  ( SELECT DISTINCT WORKERSERIAL FROM GTT_PISPAYSLIP_ED_BIRLA )
    AND TO_NUMBER(YEARMONTH) >= TO_NUMBER('202004')
    AND TO_NUMBER(YEARMONTH) <= TO_NUMBER('202004')
    GROUP BY A.COMPANYCODE,A.DIVISIONCODE, A.TOKENNO,A.UNITCODE, A.DEPARTMENTCODE, A.CATEGORYCODE, A.GRADECODE, A.WORKERSERIAL
)
UNPIVOT
(
    COMPONENTVALUE
    FOR COMPONENTCODE IN (SPL_ALLW,PERS_ALLW,OT_RT)
)

--GENERAL 

PAYSLIP NO:
EMP CODE:
EMP NAME:
DESIGNATION:
DEPARTMENT:
DATE OF BIRTH:
DATE OF JOINING:
TOTAL PAY DAYS:


SELECT COMPANYCODE, DIVISIONCODE, YEARMONTH, UNITCODE, DEPARTMENTCODE, CATEGORYCODE, GRADECODE,
WORKERSERIAL, TOKENNO, COMPONENTCODE,COMPONENTVALUE, 
DECODE(COMPONENTCODE,'EMPCODE','EMP CODE','EMPLOYEENAME','EMP NAME','DESIG','DESIGNATION','DPMT','DEPARTMENT','DATEOFBIRTH','DATE OF BIRTH','DATEOFJOIN','DATE OF JOINING') COMPONENTSHORTNAME,
1 PHASE, 
DECODE(COMPONENTCODE,'EMPCODE',1,'EMPLOYEENAME',2,'DESIG',3,'DPMT',4,'DATEOFBIRTH',5,'DATEOFJOIN',6)  CALCULATIONINDEX,COMPONENTTYPE FROM 
(
    SELECT A.COMPANYCODE,A.DIVISIONCODE, A.TOKENNO,A.YEARMONTH, A.UNITCODE, A.DEPARTMENTCODE, A.CATEGORYCODE, A.GRADECODE, A.WORKERSERIAL,
    'GENERAL' COMPONENTTYPE,B.TOKENNO EMPCODE, B.EMPLOYEENAME, C.DESIGNATIONDESC DESIG, D.DEPARTMENTDESC DPMT,
    TO_CHAR(B.DATEOFBIRTH,'DD/MM/YYYY') DATEOFBIRTH,TO_CHAR(B.DATEOFJOIN,'DD/MM/YYYY') DATEOFJOIN --,
--    B.PFNO,B.ESINO,B.BANKACCNUMBER,B.UANNO
    FROM 
    (
        SELECT DISTINCT COMPANYCODE, DIVISIONCODE, YEARMONTH, UNITCODE, DEPARTMENTCODE, 
        CATEGORYCODE, GRADECODE, WORKERSERIAL, TOKENNO 
        FROM GTT_PISPAYSLIP_ED_BIRLA
    ) A, PISEMPLOYEEMASTER B, PISDESIGNATIONMASTER C, PISDEPARTMENTMASTER D
    WHERE A.COMPANYCODE=B.COMPANYCODE
    AND A.DIVISIONCODE=B.DIVISIONCODE
    AND A.TOKENNO=B.TOKENNO
    AND B.COMPANYCODE=C.COMPANYCODE
    AND B.DIVISIONCODE=C.DIVISIONCODE
    AND B.DESIGNATIONCODE=C.DESIGNATIONCODE
    AND B.COMPANYCODE=D.COMPANYCODE
    AND B.DIVISIONCODE=D.DIVISIONCODE
    AND B.DEPARTMENTCODE=D.DEPARTMENTCODE
)
UNPIVOT
(
    COMPONENTVALUE
    FOR COMPONENTCODE IN (EMPCODE,EMPLOYEENAME,DESIG,DPMT,DATEOFBIRTH,DATEOFJOIN)
)

--GENERAL 2

QTR NO.:
PF NO.
ESI NO:
PENSION NO.:
PAN NO.:
GRATUITY NO.:
LEAVE ENCASH DAYS:



SELECT COMPANYCODE, DIVISIONCODE, YEARMONTH, UNITCODE, DEPARTMENTCODE, CATEGORYCODE, GRADECODE,
WORKERSERIAL, TOKENNO, COMPONENTCODE,COMPONENTVALUE, 
DECODE(COMPONENTCODE,'QTR_NO','QTR NO.','PFNO','PF NO.','ESINO','ESI NO','PENSIONNO','PENSION NO.','PANCARDNO','PAN NO.','GRATUITYNO','GRATUITY NO.','LEAVE_ENCASH_DAYS','LEAVE ENCASH DAYS') COMPONENTSHORTNAME,
1 PHASE, 
DECODE(COMPONENTCODE,'QTR_NO',1,'PFNO',2,'ESINO',3,'PENSIONNO',4,'PANCARDNO',5,'GRATUITYNO',6,'LEAVE_ENCASH_DAYS',7)  CALCULATIONINDEX,COMPONENTTYPE FROM 
(
    SELECT A.COMPANYCODE,A.DIVISIONCODE, A.TOKENNO,A.YEARMONTH, A.UNITCODE, A.DEPARTMENTCODE, A.CATEGORYCODE, A.GRADECODE, A.WORKERSERIAL,
    'GENERAL1' COMPONENTTYPE,NULL QTR_NO, B.PFNO, B.ESINO,B.PENSIONNO PENSIONNO,B.PANCARDNO, 'GRATUITYNO' GRATUITYNO, NULL LEAVE_ENCASH_DAYS
    FROM 
    (
        SELECT DISTINCT COMPANYCODE, DIVISIONCODE, YEARMONTH, UNITCODE, DEPARTMENTCODE, 
        CATEGORYCODE, GRADECODE, WORKERSERIAL, TOKENNO 
        FROM GTT_PISPAYSLIP_ED_BIRLA
    ) A, PISEMPLOYEEMASTER B, PISDESIGNATIONMASTER C, PISDEPARTMENTMASTER D
    WHERE A.COMPANYCODE=B.COMPANYCODE
    AND A.DIVISIONCODE=B.DIVISIONCODE
    AND A.TOKENNO=B.TOKENNO
    AND B.COMPANYCODE=C.COMPANYCODE
    AND B.DIVISIONCODE=C.DIVISIONCODE
    AND B.DESIGNATIONCODE=C.DESIGNATIONCODE
    AND B.COMPANYCODE=D.COMPANYCODE
    AND B.DIVISIONCODE=D.DIVISIONCODE
    AND B.DEPARTMENTCODE=D.DEPARTMENTCODE
)
UNPIVOT
(
    COMPONENTVALUE
    FOR COMPONENTCODE IN (QTR_NO,PFNO,ESINO,PENSIONNO,PANCARDNO,GRATUITYNO,LEAVE_ENCASH_DAYS)
)

--GENERAL  3

BANK NAME:
BANK A/C NO.:
PERSONAL AREA:
SUB AREA:
GROUP:
SUB GROUP:




SELECT COMPANYCODE, DIVISIONCODE, YEARMONTH, UNITCODE, DEPARTMENTCODE, CATEGORYCODE, GRADECODE,
WORKERSERIAL, TOKENNO, COMPONENTCODE,COMPONENTVALUE, 
DECODE(COMPONENTCODE,'BANK_NAME','BANK NAME','BANKACCNUMBER','BANK A/C NO.','PERSONAL_AREA','PERSONAL AREA','SUB_AREA','SUB AREA','GROUP_NAME','GROUP','SUBGROUP_NAME','SUB GROUP') COMPONENTSHORTNAME,
1 PHASE, 
DECODE(COMPONENTCODE,'BANK_NAME',1,'BANKACCNUMBER',2,'PERSONAL_AREA',3,'SUB_AREA',4,'GROUP_NAME',5,'SUBGROUP_NAME',6)  CALCULATIONINDEX,COMPONENTTYPE FROM 
(
    SELECT A.COMPANYCODE,A.DIVISIONCODE, A.TOKENNO,A.YEARMONTH, A.UNITCODE, A.DEPARTMENTCODE, A.CATEGORYCODE, A.GRADECODE, A.WORKERSERIAL,
    'GENERAL2' COMPONENTTYPE,'BANK_NAME' BANK_NAME, B.BANKACCNUMBER , 'PERSONAL_AREA' PERSONAL_AREA,'SUB_AREA' SUB_AREA, 'GROUP_NAME' GROUP_NAME, 'SUBGROUP_NAME' SUBGROUP_NAME
    FROM 
    (
        SELECT DISTINCT COMPANYCODE, DIVISIONCODE, YEARMONTH, UNITCODE, DEPARTMENTCODE, 
        CATEGORYCODE, GRADECODE, WORKERSERIAL, TOKENNO 
        FROM GTT_PISPAYSLIP_ED_BIRLA
    ) A, PISEMPLOYEEMASTER B, PISDESIGNATIONMASTER C, PISDEPARTMENTMASTER D
    WHERE A.COMPANYCODE=B.COMPANYCODE
    AND A.DIVISIONCODE=B.DIVISIONCODE
    AND A.TOKENNO=B.TOKENNO
    AND B.COMPANYCODE=C.COMPANYCODE
    AND B.DIVISIONCODE=C.DIVISIONCODE
    AND B.DESIGNATIONCODE=C.DESIGNATIONCODE
    AND B.COMPANYCODE=D.COMPANYCODE
    AND B.DIVISIONCODE=D.DIVISIONCODE
    AND B.DEPARTMENTCODE=D.DEPARTMENTCODE
)
UNPIVOT
(
    COMPONENTVALUE
    FOR COMPONENTCODE IN (BANK_NAME,BANKACCNUMBER,PERSONAL_AREA,SUB_AREA,GROUP_NAME,SUBGROUP_NAME)
)

select * from (
   select times_purchased, state_code
   from customers t
)
pivot 
(
   count(state_code)
   for state_code in ('NY','CT','NJ','FL','MO')
)
order by times_purchased

SELECT * FROM (

SELECT A.TOKENNO,B.YEARCODE,CALENDARYEAR,A.YEARMONTH,A.LEAVECODE,A.LV_TAKEN,A.LV_BAL,ENTITLEMENTS,CARRYFORWARD FROM
(
    SELECT * FROM GBL_PISLEAVEBALANCE
) A,
(   
    SELECT * FROM  PISLEAVEENTITLEMENT
    WHERE YEARCODE='2019-2020'
) B
WHERE A.COMPANYCODE=B.COMPANYCODE
AND A.DIVISIONCODE=B.DIVISIONCODE
AND A.LEAVECODE	= B.LEAVECODE	
AND A.TOKENNO=B.TOKENNO

)
pivot 
(
   MAX(LV_BAL)
   for LEAVECODE in ('PL' AS PL,'SL' AS SL)
)


select value
from
(
    (
        select
            'a' v1,
            'e' v2,
            'i' v3,
            'o' v4,
            'u' v5
        from dual
    )
    unpivot
    (
        value
        for value_type in
            (v1,v2,v3,v4,v5)
    )
)
/

SELECT * FROM 
(   
    SELECT *  FROM 
    (
        SELECT A.COMPANYCODE, A.DIVISIONCODE,A.TOKENNO,B.YEARCODE,CALENDARYEAR,A.YEARMONTH,A.LEAVECODE,A.LV_TAKEN AVL,A.LV_BAL BAL,ENTITLEMENTS ERN FROM
        (
            SELECT * FROM GBL_PISLEAVEBALANCE
        ) A,
        (   
            SELECT * FROM  PISLEAVEENTITLEMENT
            WHERE YEARCODE='2019-2020'
        ) B
        WHERE A.COMPANYCODE=B.COMPANYCODE
        AND A.DIVISIONCODE=B.DIVISIONCODE
        AND A.LEAVECODE	= B.LEAVECODE	
        AND A.TOKENNO=B.TOKENNO
    )
    UNPIVOT 
    (
       VALUE
       FOR COMPONENTNAME IN (AVL,BAL,ERN)
    )
)
PIVOT 
(
   MAX(VALUE)
   FOR LEAVECODE IN ('PL' AS PL,'SL' AS SL)
)

DROP TABLE GTT_PISPAYSLIP_ED CASCADE CONSTRAINTS;

CREATE GLOBAL TEMPORARY TABLE GTT_PISPAYSLIP_ED
(
  COMPANYCODE         VARCHAR2(10 BYTE),
  DIVISIONCODE        VARCHAR2(10 BYTE),
  YEARMONTH           VARCHAR2(10 BYTE),
  UNITCODE            VARCHAR2(10 BYTE),
  DEPARTMENTCODE      VARCHAR2(10 BYTE),
  CATEGORYCODE        VARCHAR2(20 BYTE),
  GRADECODE           VARCHAR2(10 BYTE),
  WORKERSERIAL        VARCHAR2(10 BYTE),
  TOKENNO             VARCHAR2(20 BYTE),
  COMPONENTCODE       VARCHAR2(20 BYTE),
  COMPONENTVALUE      NUMBER(10,2),
  COMPONENTSHORTNAME  VARCHAR2(75 BYTE),
  PHASE               NUMBER(4),
  CALCULATIONINDEX    NUMBER(10),
  COMPONENTTYPE       VARCHAR2(50 BYTE),
  COMPANYNAME         VARCHAR2(100 BYTE),
  DIVISIONNAME        VARCHAR2(100 BYTE),
  REPORTHEADER        VARCHAR2(150 BYTE)
)
ON COMMIT PRESERVE ROWS

select * from PFLOANAPPLICATION



SELECT PFNO ,WORKERSERIAL,NVL(TOKENNO,'XXXXX') TOKENNO,NVL(EMPLOYEENAME,'XXXXXX') EMPLOYEENAME,
MODULE PROJNAME FROM (SELECT * FROM PFEMPLOYEEMASTER ORDER BY TOKENNO) 
WHERE COMPANYCODE = 'NJ0002'
AND DIVISIONCODE = '0010'
AND TOKENNO LIKE '%053'
AND EMPLOYEESTATUS = 'ACTIVE' 
AND ROWNUM=1 

ORDER BY TOKENNO



SELECT COMPANYCODE, DIVISIONCODE, EMPLOYEECOMPANYCODE, EMPLOYEEDIVISIONCODE, YEARCODE, YEARMONTH, CATEGORYCODE, GRADECODE, 
PFNO, WORKERSERIAL, TOKENNO, LOANCODE, TO_CHAR(LOANDATE,'DD/MM/YYYY') LOANDATE, LOANTYPE, AMOUNT, INTERESTPERCENTAGE, 
NOOFINSTALLMENTS, AGAINSTCOMPONENT, OPENINGBALANCE, RATIOPERCENT, COMPONENTAMOUNT, CLOSINGBALANCE, ACTUALLOANAMOUNT,
TO_CHAR(ACTUALLOANDATE,'DD/MM/YYYY') ACTUALLOANDATE, COMMITEDRECOVERYPERIOD, LOANCLAIMAMOUNT, INTERESTDEDNMONTHLY, LOANAMOUNTADJUSTED, LOANINTAMOUNTADJUSTED, 
TO_CHAR(AGAINSTLOANDATE,'DD/MM/YYYY') AGAINSTLOANDATE, AGAINSTLOANCODE, PAYABLEAMOUNT, APPLICATIONNO, AMOUNTINHAND, INTERESTAMOUNT, CAPITALINSTALLMENTAMT,
INTERESTINSTALLMENTAMT, REPAYCAPITAL, REPAYINTEREST,TO_CHAR(ADJUSTMENTDATE,'DD/MM/YYYY') ADJUSTMENTDATE, REMARKS, DEPARTMENTCODE,TO_CHAR(FORTNIGHTSTARTDATE,'DD/MM/YYYY') FORTNIGHTSTARTDATE,
LOANNL, NEXTLOAN, ACTUALINTERESTAMOUNT, NEWINTERESTAMOUNT,TO_CHAR(DEDUCTIONSTARTDATE,'DD/MM/YYYY') DEDUCTIONSTARTDATE, INTERESTBALANCEAMOUNT, CAPITALBALANCEAMOUNT,
CAPITALINSTALLMENTAMOUNT, INTERESTINSTALLMENTAMOUNT,TO_CHAR(ADJUSTEDLOANDATE,'DD/MM/YYYY') ADJUSTEDLOANDATE, TOTALEMIAMOUNT, PF_E, PF_C, VPF, MINBALANCE, ACTUALBALANCE,
MODULE, PFGROSS, VOUCHERNO,TO_CHAR(VOUCHERDATE,'DD/MM/YYYY') VOUCHERDATE, SYSTEMVOUCHERNO,TO_CHAR(SYSTEMVOUCHERDATE,'DD/MM/YYYY') SYSTEMVOUCHERDATE, CHEQUENO,TO_CHAR(CHEQUEDATE,'DD/MM/YYYY') CHEQUEDATE, ELIGIBLE, USERNAME,
SYSROWID, LOANCF, SANCTIONEDAMOUNT,PREV_LOAN_CAP_EMI, CURR_INT_EMI, CURR_CAP_EMI, PREV_LOAN_INT_EMI
, ceil(NOOFINSTALLMENTS/25) SANCTIONYEAR
FROM PFLOANAPPLICATION WHERE COMPANYCODE = 'NJ0002'

CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION FN_GET_PARAMVALUE
(
    P_PARAMS VARCHAR2,
    P_PARAMNAME VARCHAR2
)
RETURN VARCHAR2
AS
LV_RESULT   VARCHAR2(4000); 
BEGIN
    LV_RESULT := NULL;
    --SELECT FN_GET_PARAMVALUE('COMPANYCODE:0001~DIVISIONCODE:0002','COMPANYCODE') FROM DUAL
 
    SELECT PARAMVALUE INTO LV_RESULT FROM (
    SELECT REC1,SUBSTR(REC1,0,INSTR(REC1,':')-1) PARAMNAME,
        SUBSTR(REC1,INSTR(REC1,':')+1, LENGTH(REC1)) PARAMVALUE 
        FROM 
        (
            select regexp_substr(P_PARAMS,'[^~]+', 1, level) REC1
            from dual 
            connect BY regexp_substr(P_PARAMS, '[^~]+', 1, level) 
            is not null
        ) 
    )
    WHERE PARAMNAME=P_PARAMNAME;
    
    RETURN LV_RESULT;
EXCEPTION WHEN OTHERS THEN   
    LV_RESULT := NULL; 
    
    RETURN LV_RESULT;
END;
/

CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION FN_GET_QRYSTRING
(
    P_PARAMS VARCHAR2,
    P_QUERY VARCHAR2
)
RETURN VARCHAR2
AS
LV_RESULT   VARCHAR2(4000); 
BEGIN
    LV_RESULT := P_QUERY;
        
    --LV_PARAMS := 'COMPANYCODE:0001~DIVISIONCODE:0002';
    --LV_QRY := 'SELECT <<COMPANYCODE>>,<<DIVISIONCODE>> FROM DUAL';
--SELECT FN_GET_QRYSTRING('COMPANYCODE:0001~DIVISIONCODE:0002','SELECT <<COMPANYCODE>>,<<DIVISIONCODE>> FROM DUAL') FROM DUAL

    FOR C1 IN 
    (  
        SELECT REC1,SUBSTR(REC1,0,INSTR(REC1,':')-1) PARAMNAME,
        SUBSTR(REC1,INSTR(REC1,':')+1, LENGTH(REC1)) PARAMVALUE 
        FROM 
        (
            SELECT REGEXP_SUBSTR(P_PARAMS,'[^~]+', 1, LEVEL) REC1
            FROM DUAL 
            CONNECT BY REGEXP_SUBSTR(P_PARAMS, '[^~]+', 1, LEVEL) 
            IS NOT NULL
        ) 
    )
    LOOP
        LV_RESULT := REPLACE(LV_RESULT,'<<'||C1.PARAMNAME||'>>',C1.PARAMVALUE);
    END LOOP; 
    RETURN LV_RESULT;
END;
/
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

DECLARE

LV_PARAMS VARCHAR2(1000);
LV_QRY VARCHAR2(1000);

BEGIN
LV_PARAMS := 'COMPANYCODE:0001~DIVISIONCODE:0002';
LV_QRY := 'SELECT <<COMPANYCODE>>,<<DIVISIONCODE>> FROM DUAL';
--
--select regexp_substr('COMPANYCODE:0001~DIVISIONCODE:0002','[^~]+', 1, level) REC1
--   from dual 
--   connect BY regexp_substr('COMPANYCODE:0001~DIVISIONCODE:0002', '[^~]+', 1, level) 
--   is not null
--   
--   
--select regexp_substr('COMPANYCODE:0001','[^:]+', 1, level) REC1
--   from dual 
--   connect BY regexp_substr('COMPANYCODE:0001', '[^:]+', 1, level) 
--   is not null
--   

DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(LV_PARAMS);
DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(LV_QRY);
FOR C1 IN (  
    SELECT REC1,SUBSTR(REC1,0,INSTR(REC1,':')-1) PARAMNAME,
    SUBSTR(REC1,INSTR(REC1,':')+1, LENGTH(REC1)) PARAMVALUE 
    FROM 
    (
        select regexp_substr(LV_PARAMS,'[^~]+', 1, level) REC1
        from dual 
        connect BY regexp_substr(LV_PARAMS, '[^~]+', 1, level) 
        is not null
    ) 
)
LOOP
    LV_QRY := REPLACE(LV_QRY,'<<'||C1.PARAMNAME||'>>',C1.PARAMVALUE);
END LOOP;  

DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(LV_QRY);
--   
--   SELECT SUBSTR('DIVISIONCODE:0002',INSTR('DIVISIONCODE:0002',':')+1, LENGTH('DIVISIONCODE:0002')) PARAMVALUE FROM DUAL
--   
--   SELECT SUBSTR('DIVISIONCODE:0002',0,INSTR('DIVISIONCODE:0002',':')-1) PARAMNAME FROM DUAL
END;

SELECT PARAMVALUE FROM (
SELECT REC1,SUBSTR(REC1,0,INSTR(REC1,':')-1) PARAMNAME,
    SUBSTR(REC1,INSTR(REC1,':')+1, LENGTH(REC1)) PARAMVALUE 
    FROM 
    (
        select regexp_substr('COMPANYCODE:0001~DIVISIONCODE:0002','[^~]+', 1, level) REC1
        from dual 
        connect BY regexp_substr('COMPANYCODE:0001~DIVISIONCODE:0002', '[^~]+', 1, level) 
        is not null
    ) 
)
WHERE PARAMNAME='COMPANYCODE'

--KANCO COMPONENT ASSIGNMENT DATA NOT FETCHING IN EDIT MODE

--UNITCODE = HO

SELECT * FROM 
(
    SELECT EMPMAST.COMPANYCODE,EMPMAST.DIVISIONCODE,ASSIGN.SYSROWID,ASSIGN.YEARCODE,ASSIGN.YEARMONTH,EMPMAST.UNITCODE,
    EMPMAST.CATEGORYCODE,EMPMAST.GRADECODE,EMPMAST.WORKERSERIAL,EMPMAST.TOKENNO,EMPMAST.EMPLOYEENAME,EMPMAST.DEPARTMENTCODE,
    DEPT.DEPARTMENTDESC,ASSIGN.BASIC,ASSIGN.DA_RATA,ASSIGN.DA_AMOUNT,ASSIGN.VDA_RATE,ASSIGN.VDA,ASSIGN.HRA_FIX,ASSIGN.HRA_PER,
    ASSIGN.TIFFN_ALLW,ASSIGN.SHIFT_ALLW,ASSIGN.TRNP_ALLW,ASSIGN.SPCL_ALLW,ASSIGN.EDUC_ALLW,ASSIGN.SOFT_FURNS,ASSIGN.LV_ENCASH,
    ASSIGN.ENTMT_ALLW,ASSIGN.PRFRM_BONUS,ASSIGN.EX_GRATIA,ASSIGN.KIT_ALLW,ASSIGN.OTH_ALLW_1,ASSIGN.OTH_ALLW_2,ASSIGN.OTH_ALLW_TM,
    ASSIGN.ADHOC_DA,ASSIGN.OTH_DEDN_TM,ASSIGN.RENT   
    FROM PISEMPLOYEEMASTER EMPMAST, --PISDEPARTMENTMASTER DEPT,         
    (         
        SELECT *           
        FROM PISCOMPONENTASSIGNMENT          
        WHERE COMPANYCODE='KT0081'            
        AND DIVISIONCODE='0001'            
        AND TRANSACTIONTYPE='ASSIGNMENT'            
        AND WORKERSERIAL||YEARMONTH IN 
        (                                             
            SELECT WORKERSERIAL||MAX(YEARMONTH) 
            FROM PISCOMPONENTASSIGNMENT                                              
            WHERE COMPANYCODE='KT0081' AND DIVISIONCODE='0001'                                                
            AND TO_NUMBER(YEARMONTH)<=TO_NUMBER('202004')                                                
            AND TRANSACTIONTYPE='ASSIGNMENT'                                             
            GROUP BY WORKERSERIAL                                           
        )        
    ) ASSIGN  
    WHERE EMPMAST.COMPANYCODE=DEPT.COMPANYCODE    
    AND EMPMAST.DIVISIONCODE=DEPT.DIVISIONCODE    
    AND EMPMAST.DEPARTMENTCODE=DEPT.DEPARTMENTCODE    
    AND EMPMAST.COMPANYCODE=ASSIGN.COMPANYCODE(+)    
    AND EMPMAST.DIVISIONCODE=ASSIGN.DIVISIONCODE(+)    
    AND EMPMAST.TOKENNO=ASSIGN.TOKENNO(+)    
    AND EMPMAST.WORKERSERIAL=ASSIGN.WORKERSERIAL(+)    
    AND EMPMAST.COMPANYCODE='KT0081'    
    AND EMPMAST.DIVISIONCODE='0001'    
    AND EMPMAST.UNITCODE='HO'    
    AND EMPMAST.CATEGORYCODE='GMS'    
    AND EMPMAST.GRADECODE='GMS'    
--    AND TO_NUMBER(TO_CHAR(EMPMAST.DATEOFJOIN,'YYYYMM'))<=TO_NUMBER('202004')    
--    AND TO_NUMBER(NVL(TO_CHAR(EMPMAST.STATUSDATE,'YYYYMM'),NVL(TO_CHAR(EMPMAST.EXTENDEDRETIREDATE,'YYYYMM'),'202004')))>=TO_NUMBER('202004') 
) 
ORDER BY TOKENNO 

SELECT * FROM PISEMPLOYEEMASTER
WHERE CATEGORYCODE='GMS'
AND TOKENNO = '00024'

SELECT ROUND(nvl(B.AMOUNT,0) * 100/NVL(A.AMOUNT,1)) PERCENTAGE FROM
(   
SELECT PFNO,LOANDATE,LOANCODE, AMOUNT FROM PFLOANTRANSACTION
WHERE COMPANYCODE=P_COMPCODE
--AND DIVISIONCODE=P_DIVCODE
AND LOANCODE=P_LOANCODE
AND PFNO=P_PFNO
AND LOANDATE=
(
SELECT MAX(LOANDATE) FROM PFLOANTRANSACTION
WHERE COMPANYCODE=P_COMPCODE
--AND DIVISIONCODE =P_DIVCODE
AND LOANCODE=P_LOANCODE
AND PFNO=P_PFNO
)

) A,
( 
SELECT PFNO,LOANDATE,LOANCODE,SUM(CASE WHEN TRANSACTIONTYPE='REPAY' THEN REPAYCAPITAL ELSE AMOUNT END) AMOUNT FROM PFLOANBREAKUP
WHERE COMPANYCODE=P_COMPCODE
AND DIVISIONCODE=P_DIVCODE
AND LOANCODE=P_LOANCODE
AND PFNO=P_PFNO
AND TRANSACTIONTYPE IN ('CAPITAL','REPAYCAP','REPAY')
AND LOANDATE=
(
    SELECT MAX(LOANDATE) FROM PFLOANTRANSACTION
    WHERE COMPANYCODE=P_COMPCODE
    --AND DIVISIONCODE =P_DIVCODE
    AND LOANCODE=P_LOANCODE
    AND PFNO=P_PFNO
)
GROUP BY PFNO,LOANDATE,LOANCODE
) B
WHERE A.PFNO =B.PFNO(+)
AND A.LOANDATE=B.LOANDATE(+)
AND A.LOANCODE=B.LOANCODE(+);

SELECT * FROM (
SELECT '0002' COMPANYCODE,'0010' DIVISIONCODE,'2020-2021' YEARCODE,
NVL(D.PFNO,P.PFNO) PFNO,NVL(D.TOKENNO,P.TOKENNO) TOKENNO,NVL(D.WORKERSERIAL,P.WORKERSERIAL) WORKERSERIAL,TO_CHAR(NVL(D.LOANDATE,P.LOANDATE),'DD/MM/YYYY') LOANDATE,NVL(D.LOANCODE,P.LOANCODE) LOANCODE,
NVL(D.PARAM_NAME,P.PARAM_NAME) PARAM_NAME,NVL(D.PF_E,P.PF_E) PF_E,NVL(D.PF_C,P.PF_C) PF_C,NVL( D.VPF,P.VPF) VPF, NVL(D.OTHER,P.OTHER) OTHER,'M' OPERATIONMODE,P.ISELLIGIBLE,P.REMARKS
FROM GTT_LOANSANCTION_PRAM P,LOANSANCTION_DETAILS D
WHERE P.PFNO=D.PFNO(+)
AND P.COMPANYCODE=D.COMPANYCODE(+)
AND P.DIVISIONCODE=D.DIVISIONCODE(+)
AND P.LOANCODE=D.LOANCODE(+)
AND P.LOANDATE=D.LOANDATE(+)
AND P.PARAM_NAME=D.PARAM_NAME(+)
ORDER BY TABINDEX
)
WHERE PF_E IS NOT NULL OR PF_C IS NOT NULL OR VPF IS NOT NULL OR OTHER IS NOT NULL OR ISELLIGIBLE IS NOT NULL OR REMARKS IS NOT NULL

  QUALITY_GROUP_CODE  VARCHAR2(1000 BYTE)       NOT NULL,
  CHANNELCODE         VARCHAR2(100 BYTE)        NOT NULL,
  ACCODE              VARCHAR2(50 BYTE),
  SYSROWID            VARCHAR2(50 BYTE)
)

DROP TABLE PISSALARY_POSTINGDATA CASCADE CONSTRAINTS;

CREATE TABLE PISSALARY_POSTINGDATA
(
  COMPANYCODE       VARCHAR2(10 BYTE),
  DIVISIONCODE      VARCHAR2(10 BYTE),
  PERIODFROM        DATE,
  PERIODTO          DATE,
  ACCODE            VARCHAR2(10 BYTE),
  ACHEAD            VARCHAR2(200 BYTE),
  DRCR              VARCHAR2(10 BYTE),
  AMOUNT            NUMBER(11,2),
  ACCOSTCENTRECODE  VARCHAR2(10 BYTE),
  CATEGORYCODE      VARCHAR2(100 BYTE),
  VORD              VARCHAR2(2 BYTE),
  UNITCODE          VARCHAR2(10 BYTE),
  GRADECODE         VARCHAR2(10 BYTE)
)



DROP TABLE PISSALARY_POSTINGDATA_CC CASCADE CONSTRAINTS;

CREATE TABLE PISSALARY_POSTINGDATA_CC
(
  COMPANYCODE       VARCHAR2(10 BYTE),
  DIVISIONCODE      VARCHAR2(10 BYTE),
  PERIODFROM        DATE,
  PERIODTO          DATE,
  ACCODE            VARCHAR2(10 BYTE),
  ACHEAD            VARCHAR2(200 BYTE),
  DRCR              VARCHAR2(10 BYTE),
  AMOUNT            NUMBER(11,2),
  ACCOSTCENTRECODE  VARCHAR2(10 BYTE),
  CATEGORYCODE      VARCHAR2(100 BYTE),
  VORD              VARCHAR2(2 BYTE),
  UNITCODE          VARCHAR2(10 BYTE),
  GRADECODE         VARCHAR2(10 BYTE)
)

select fn_drcr_mismatch('0001','001', '2020-2021','001/PIS/M/20-21/000000001')  from dual

select systemvoucherno,sum(decode(drcr,'D',amount,-amount)) as balance
    from acvoucherdetails
    where companycode = '0001'
      and divisioncode = '001'
      and yearcode = '2020-2021'
      and SYSTEMVOUCHERNO = '001/PIS/M/20-21/000000001'
    group by systemvoucherno
    
    having sum(decode(drcr,'D',amount,-amount)) <> 0 
    
    

   exec prc_delete_systemvoucher('0001','001', '2020-2021','001/PIS/M/20-21/000000001','FORCED');
    
   exec prc_delete_systemvoucher('0001','001', '2020-2021','001/PIS/M/20-21/000000002','FORCED');
    
   exec prc_delete_systemvoucher('0001','001', '2020-2021','001/PIS/M/20-21/000000003','FORCED');
   
   exec prc_delete_systemvoucher('0001','001', '2020-2021','001/PIS/M/20-21/000000004','FORCED');
    
  
    select * from acvoucher
    where systemvoucherno = '001/PIS/M/20-21/000000002';
    
    select * from acvoucherdetails_entry
    where systemvoucherno = '001/PIS/M/20-21/000000004';
    
    
    
     select fn_autogen_params('0001','001', '2020-2021','AC_SYS_VOUCHERNO_PIS_STAFF','30/04/2020') -- Change by Bishwanath on 10/12/2019 to add arrear posting
            lv_systemvoucherno
            from dual;
            


select distinct systemvoucherno, voucherno, to_char(voucherdate,'dd/mm/yyyy') voucherdate
--into lv_systemvoucherno, lv_voucherno, lv_voucherdate
from acvoucher
where companycode = '0001'
and divisioncode = '001'
and yearcode = '2020-2021'
and voucherdate = to_date('30/04/2020','dd/mm/yyyy')
--and documenttype = 'PIS PAYROLL'
--and documenttype = 'PIS ' || p_categorycode || ' PAYROLL'
--and narration like '%' || '' || '%FROM ' || '01/04/2020' || ' TO ' || '30/04/2020' || '%'
and substr(voucherno,1,8) = 
(
    select substr(prefix,1,8) prefix  
    from sys_autogen_params 
    where companycode= '0001' 
    and divisioncode = '001' 
    and yearcode = '2020-2021'  
    --and param_name = 'AC_VOUCHERNO_PIS_STAFF'  Change by Bishwanath on 10/12/2019 to add arrear posting
    and param_name = 'AC_SYS_VOUCHERNO_PIS_STAFF'
);

exec prcpis_post_to_acc('0001','001','SALARY PROCESS','202004','001','','','')

select * from sys_gbl_procoutput_info

[JOURNAL NO : 001/PIS/2021/00001, JOURNAL DATE : 30-APR-20 SYSTEM VOUCHER NUMBER GENERATED: 001/PIS/M/20-21/000000001 Dated : 25-JUL-20]

select * from acvoucherdetails

PARAM_NAME='AC_VOUCHERNO_PIS_STAFF_ARR'

select fn_drcr_mismatch('0001','001', '2020-2021','001/PIS/M/20-21/000000001')  from dual

select systemvoucherno,sum(decode(drcr,'D',amount,-amount)) as balance
    from acvoucherdetails
    where companycode = '0001'
      and divisioncode = '001'
      and yearcode = '2020-2021'
      and SYSTEMVOUCHERNO = '001/PIS/M/20-21/000000001'
    group by systemvoucherno
    having sum(decode(drcr,'D',amount,-amount)) <> 0 
    
    
    
    insert into acvoucher
    (companycode, divisioncode, yearcode, 
     voucherno, voucherdate, vouchertype, 
     systemvoucherno, systemvoucherdate, voucheramount, 
     narration, automanualmark, preparedby, prepareddate, 
     modulename, documenttype, manualvoucherno, 
     username, sysrowid,vouchernature,liabilitytype
    )
    
    select             
     '0001','001' p_divisioncode,'2020-2021' lv_yearcode,
     '001/PIS/2021/00001' lv_voucherno, to_date('30/04/2020','dd/mm/yyyy'),'JOURNAL' as vouchertype,
     '001/PIS/M/20-21/000000001' lv_systemvoucherno, to_date('25/05/2020','dd/mm/yyyy'), 0 as voucheramount, 
     'POSTING' as narration, 'AUTO VOUCHER' as automanualmark,'prcpis_post_to_acc' as preparedby, trunc(sysdate) as prepareddate,
     --'PIS' as modulename, 'PIS ' || p_categorycode || ' PAYROLL' as documenttype, null manualvoucherno,  --  Change by Bishwanath on 11/12/2019 to add arrear posting
     'PIS' as modulename, 'PIS ' as documenttype, null manualvoucherno,           
     'SWT' username,fn_generate_sysrowid(),null vouchernature,null liabilitytype
    from dual;

--BAGGAGE WEB
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

SELECT ACCODE,SUM(VOUCHERAMOUNT) AS VOUCHERAMOUNT,SUM(TDSAMOUNT) AS TDSAMOUNT
FROM (
SELECT A.ACCODE,SUM(DECODE(A.DRCR,'D',A.AMOUNT,-A.AMOUNT)) AS VOUCHERAMOUNT,0.00 AS TDSAMOUNT
FROM ACVOUCHERDETAILS A, ACACLEDGER B
WHERE a.companycode = '0001'
  and a.divisioncode = '001'
  and a.yearcode = '2020-2021'
  and a.companycode = b.companycode
  and A.SYSTEMVOUCHERNO = '001/PIS/M/20-21/000000001'
  AND A.ACCODE=B.ACCODE
  AND B.GROUPTYPE IN ('TDS')
GROUP BY A.ACCODE
UNION ALL
SELECT A.ACCODE,0.00 AS VOUCHERAMOUNT,SUM(DECODE(A.DRCR,'D',A.TOTALTDSAMOUNT,-A.TOTALTDSAMOUNT)) AS TDSAMOUNT
FROM ACTDSDETAILS A, ACACLEDGER B
WHERE a.companycode = '0001'
  and a.divisioncode = '001'
  and a.yearcode = '2020-2021'
  and a.companycode = b.companycode
  and A.SYSTEMVOUCHERNO = '001/PIS/M/20-21/000000001'
  AND A.ACCODE=B.ACCODE
  AND B.GROUPTYPE IN ('TDS')
GROUP BY A.ACCODE
)
GROUP BY ACCODE
HAVING SUM(VOUCHERAMOUNT) <> SUM(TDSAMOUNT)

CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW VW_PISCOMPONENTLEDGERMAPPING 
 AS 
 
 
 SELECT COMPANYCODE, DIVISIONCODE, QUALITY_GROUP_CODE as COMPONENTCODE,  ACCODE ACCCODE 
 FROM SYS_PARAM_ACPOST_GPS 
 WHERE COMPANYCODE = '0001' AND DIVISIONCODE = '001' 
 AND  POSTING_PARAM_NAME = 'PIS SALARY POSTING TO ACCOUNTS' 
 AND  MODULENAME = 'PIS' 
 
 SELECT DISTINCT COMPANYCODE, DIVISIONCODE, COMPONENTCODE, EXPENSECODE 
            FROM PISCOMPONENTMASTER 
           WHERE COMPANYCODE = '0001' 
             AND DIVISIONCODE = '001' 
             AND  EXPENSECODE IS NOT NULL 
             
             
SELECT * FROM PISCOMPONENTMASTER      
WHERE EXPENSECODE LIKE '%114'

       


INSERT INTO PISSALARY_POSTINGDATA 
( 
  COMPANYCODE, DIVISIONCODE, PERIODFROM, PERIODTO, ACCODE, ACHEAD, DRCR, AMOUNT, ACCOSTCENTRECODE, CATEGORYCODE, UNITCODE, GRADECODE 
) 

SELECT D.COMPANYCODE,D.DIVISIONCODE, D.COMPONENTCODE, 
       TO_DATE('01/04/2020','DD/MM/YYYY') PERIODFROM,TO_DATE('30/04/2020','DD/MM/YYYY') PERIODTO, 
       C.ACCCODE, B.ACHEAD, 
       CASE                                                
            WHEN D.COMPONENTCODE = 'NETSALARY' THEN 'CR' 
            WHEN C.ACCCODE IN (SELECT DISTINCT EXPENSECODE FROM PISCOMPONENTMASTER ) THEN 'CR'  
            WHEN C.ACCCODE IN (SELECT DISTINCT ACCCODE FROM PISCOMPONENTMASTER WHERE COMPONENTCODE IN ('PF_C','FPF')) THEN 'CR' 
            WHEN D.COMPONENTTYPE = 'EARNING' THEN 'DR' 
            WHEN D.COMPONENTTYPE = 'DEDUCTION' THEN 'CR' 
            ELSE 'DR' 
        END AS DRCR, 
       FN_PISSALARY_COMP_AMT(C.COMPANYCODE,C.DIVISIONCODE,'SALARY PROCESS',C.COMPONENTCODE, '202004' , '' , '001' , '')  AMOUNT, 
       NULL ACCOSTCENTRECODE, '' CATEGORYCODE, '001' UNITCODE, '' GRADECODE 
  FROM PISCOMPONENTMASTER D, 
        ( 
          SELECT DISTINCT COMPANYCODE, DIVISIONCODE, COMPONENTCODE, ACCCODE 
            FROM VW_PISCOMPONENTLEDGERMAPPING 
           WHERE COMPANYCODE = '0001' 
             AND DIVISIONCODE = '001' 
             UNION ALL
          SELECT DISTINCT COMPANYCODE, DIVISIONCODE, COMPONENTCODE, EXPENSECODE 
            FROM PISCOMPONENTMASTER 
           WHERE COMPANYCODE = '0001' 
             AND DIVISIONCODE = '001' 
        ) C ,ACACLEDGER B 
 WHERE C.COMPANYCODE = '0001' 
   AND C.DIVISIONCODE = '001' 
   AND C.COMPANYCODE = D.COMPANYCODE 
   AND C.DIVISIONCODE = D.DIVISIONCODE 
   AND C.COMPONENTCODE=D.COMPONENTCODE 
   AND B.COMPANYCODE = C.COMPANYCODE 
   AND B.ACCODE = C.ACCCODE

INSERT INTO PISSALARY_POSTINGDATA_CC 
( 
  COMPANYCODE, DIVISIONCODE, PERIODFROM, PERIODTO, ACCODE, ACHEAD, DRCR, AMOUNT, ACCOSTCENTRECODE, CATEGORYCODE, UNITCODE, GRADECODE  
) 

SELECT D.COMPANYCODE,D.DIVISIONCODE, 
       TO_DATE('01/04/2020','DD/MM/YYYY') PERIODFROM,TO_DATE('30/04/2020','DD/MM/YYYY') PERIODTO, 
       C.ACCCODE, B.ACHEAD, 
       CASE  
            WHEN D.COMPONENTCODE = 'NETSALARY' THEN 'CR' 
            WHEN C.ACCCODE IN (SELECT DISTINCT ACCCODE FROM PISCOMPONENTMASTER WHERE COMPONENTCODE IN ('PF_C','FPF')) THEN 'CR' 
            WHEN D.COMPONENTTYPE = 'EARNING' THEN 'DR' 
            WHEN D.COMPONENTTYPE = 'DEDUCTION' THEN 'CR' 
            ELSE 'DR' 
        END AS DRCR, 
       FN_PISSALARY_COMP_AMT_CC(C.COMPANYCODE,C.DIVISIONCODE,'SALARY PROCESS',C.COMPONENTCODE, '202004' , '' , '001' , '',PT.WORKERSERIAL)  AMOUNT, 
       X.COSTCENTRECODE ACCOSTCENTRECODE, '' CATEGORYCODE, '001' UNITCODE , '' GRADECODE 
  FROM PISCOMPONENTMASTER D, PISPAYTRANSACTION PT, PISEMPLOYEEMASTER X,
        ( 
          SELECT DISTINCT COMPANYCODE, DIVISIONCODE, COMPONENTCODE, ACCCODE 
            FROM VW_PISCOMPONENTLEDGERMAPPING 
           WHERE COMPANYCODE = '0001' 
             AND DIVISIONCODE = '001' 
        ) C ,ACACLEDGER B 
 WHERE C.COMPANYCODE = '0001' 
   AND C.DIVISIONCODE = '001' 
   AND C.COMPANYCODE = D.COMPANYCODE 
   AND C.DIVISIONCODE = D.DIVISIONCODE 
   AND C.COMPONENTCODE=D.COMPONENTCODE 
   AND B.COMPANYCODE = C.COMPANYCODE 
   AND B.ACCODE = C.ACCCODE 
   AND C.COMPANYCODE = PT.COMPANYCODE 
   AND C.DIVISIONCODE = PT.DIVISIONCODE 
   AND PT.YEARMONTH = '202004' 
   AND PT.CATEGORYCODE = '' 
   AND PT.COMPANYCODE = X.COMPANYCODE 
   AND PT.DIVISIONCODE = X.DIVISIONCODE 
   AND PT.WORKERSERIAL = X.WORKERSERIAL

COMPONENTDESC		VARCHAR2(300),

select fn_drcr_mismatch('0001','001', '2020-2021','001/PIS/M/20-21/000000001') from dual

[JOURNAL NO : 001/PIS/2021/00001, JOURNAL DATE : 30-APR-20 SYSTEM VOUCHER NUMBER GENERATED: 001/PIS/M/20-21/000000001 Dated : 24-JUL-20]


select systemvoucherno,sum(decode(drcr,'D',amount,-amount)) as balance
    from acvoucherdetails
    where companycode = '0001'
      and divisioncode = '001'
      and yearcode = '2020-2021'
      and SYSTEMVOUCHERNO = '001/PIS/M/20-21/000000001'
    group by systemvoucherno
    having sum(decode(drcr,'D',amount,-amount)) <> 0 
    
select * from    acvoucherdetails where  SYSTEMVOUCHERNO = '001/PIS/M/20-21/000000001'
    
    
update BMPL_COMPONENT_LEDGER_MAPPING set
componentcode = replace(componentcode,'.','_')
where componentcode like '%.%'	


UPDATE PISCOMPONENTMASTER A SET
ACCCODE = (
    SELECT ACCCODE FROM (
    SELECT LOCATIONCODE, COMPONENTCODE, ACCCODE FROM BMPL_COMPONENT_LEDGER_MAPPING
    )
    WHERE A.DIVISIONCODE=LOCATIONCODE
    AND A.COMPONENTCODE=COMPONENTCODE
)
WHERE COMPONENTCODE IN (
SELECT DISTINCT COMPONENTCODE FROM BMPL_COMPONENT_LEDGER_MAPPING
)

INSERT INTO PISSALARY_POSTINGDATA 
( 
  COMPANYCODE, DIVISIONCODE, PERIODFROM, PERIODTO, ACCODE, ACHEAD, DRCR, AMOUNT, ACCOSTCENTRECODE, CATEGORYCODE, UNITCODE, GRADECODE 
) 

SELECT D.COMPANYCODE,D.DIVISIONCODE, 
       TO_DATE('01/04/2020','DD/MM/YYYY') PERIODFROM,TO_DATE('30/04/2020','DD/MM/YYYY') PERIODTO, 
       C.ACCCODE, B.ACHEAD, 
       CASE WHEN D.COMPONENTTYPE = 'EARNING' THEN 'DR' 
            WHEN D.COMPONENTTYPE = 'DEDUCTION' THEN 'CR' 
            WHEN D.COMPONENTCODE = 'NETSALARY' THEN 'CR' 
            WHEN C.ACCCODE IN ('SYS0599','E000072','P000180','D000109') THEN 'CR' 
            ELSE 'DR' 
        END AS DRCR, 
       FN_PISSALARY_COMP_AMT(C.COMPANYCODE,C.DIVISIONCODE,'SALARY PROCESS',C.COMPONENTCODE, '202004' , '01' , '002' , 'CIV')  AMOUNT, 
       NULL ACCOSTCENTRECODE, '01' CATEGORYCODE, '002' UNITCODE, 'CIV' GRADECODE 
  FROM PISCOMPONENTMASTER D, 
        ( 
          SELECT DISTINCT COMPANYCODE, DIVISIONCODE, COMPONENTCODE, ACCCODE 
            FROM VW_PISCOMPONENTLEDGERMAPPING 
           WHERE COMPANYCODE = '0001' 
             AND DIVISIONCODE = '001' 
        ) C ,ACACLEDGER B 
 WHERE C.COMPANYCODE = '0001' 
   AND C.DIVISIONCODE = '001' 
   AND C.COMPANYCODE = D.COMPANYCODE 
   AND C.DIVISIONCODE = D.DIVISIONCODE 
   AND C.COMPONENTCODE=D.COMPONENTCODE 
   AND B.COMPANYCODE = C.COMPANYCODE 
   AND B.ACCODE = C.ACCCODE

INSERT INTO PISSALARY_POSTINGDATA_CC 
( 
  COMPANYCODE, DIVISIONCODE, PERIODFROM, PERIODTO, ACCODE, ACHEAD, DRCR, AMOUNT, ACCOSTCENTRECODE, CATEGORYCODE, UNITCODE, GRADECODE  
) 

SELECT D.COMPANYCODE,D.DIVISIONCODE, 
       TO_DATE('01/04/2020','DD/MM/YYYY') PERIODFROM,TO_DATE('30/04/2020','DD/MM/YYYY') PERIODTO, 
       C.ACCCODE, B.ACHEAD, 
       CASE WHEN D.COMPONENTTYPE = 'EARNING' THEN 'DR' 
            WHEN D.COMPONENTTYPE = 'DEDUCTION' THEN 'CR' 
            WHEN D.COMPONENTCODE = 'NETSALARY' THEN 'CR' 
            WHEN C.ACCCODE IN ('SYS0599','E000072','P000180','D000109') THEN 'CR' 
            ELSE 'DR' 
        END AS DRCR, 
       FN_PISSALARY_COMP_AMT_CC(C.COMPANYCODE,C.DIVISIONCODE,'SALARY PROCESS',C.COMPONENTCODE, '202004' , '01' , '002' , 'CIV',PT.WORKERSERIAL)  AMOUNT, 
       X.COSTCENTRECODE ACCOSTCENTRECODE, '01' CATEGORYCODE, '002' UNITCODE , 'CIV' GRADECODE 
  FROM PISCOMPONENTMASTER D, PISPAYTRANSACTION PT, PISEMPLOYEEMASTER X,
        ( 
          SELECT DISTINCT COMPANYCODE, DIVISIONCODE, COMPONENTCODE, ACCCODE 
            FROM VW_PISCOMPONENTLEDGERMAPPING 
           WHERE COMPANYCODE = '0001' 
             AND DIVISIONCODE = '001' 
        ) C ,ACACLEDGER B 
 WHERE C.COMPANYCODE = '0001' 
   AND C.DIVISIONCODE = '001' 
   AND C.COMPANYCODE = D.COMPANYCODE 
   AND C.DIVISIONCODE = D.DIVISIONCODE 
   AND C.COMPONENTCODE=D.COMPONENTCODE 
   AND B.COMPANYCODE = C.COMPANYCODE 
   AND B.ACCODE = C.ACCCODE 
   AND C.COMPANYCODE = PT.COMPANYCODE 
   AND C.DIVISIONCODE = PT.DIVISIONCODE 
   AND PT.YEARMONTH = '202004' 
   AND PT.CATEGORYCODE = '01' 
   AND PT.COMPANYCODE = X.COMPANYCODE 
   AND PT.DIVISIONCODE = X.DIVISIONCODE 
   AND PT.WORKERSERIAL = X.WORKERSERIAL

INSERT INTO GTT_ACCASHBANKBOOKRPT 

SELECT COM.COMPANYNAME,DIV.DIVISIONNAME,TTYPE , OPACCODE, 
            OPENINGDR, OPENINGCR, NETOPENING, 
            CASE WHEN MAINACCODE IS NULL THEN OPACCODE ELSE MAINACCODE END  MAINACCODE, MAINACHEAD, YEARCODE, A.DIVISIONCODE, SYSTEMVOUCHERNO, VOUCHERTYPE, VOUCHERNO, VOUCHERDATE, 
            CHEQUENO, CHEQUEDATE, CHEQUEPAIDTO, NARRATION, 
            ACAMOUNT, ACDRCR, ACREMARKS, ACSERIALNO, 
            ACCODE , ACHEAD, SERIALNO, DRCR, AMOUNT, REMARKS, TO_DATE('01/04/2020','DD/MM/YYYY') FROMDATE, TO_DATE('31/03/2021','DD/MM/YYYY') TODATE, 
            TO_DATE(SYSDATE,'DD/MM/YYYY') RUNDATE, 'A' EX1,'A'EX2,'A'EX3,'A'EX4,'A'EX5 
 FROM 
 ( 
        SELECT 'T' TTYPE , NULL OPACCODE, 
            0 AS OPENINGDR, 0 AS OPENINGCR, 0 AS NETOPENING, 
            A.MAINACCODE, L.ACHEAD MAINACHEAD, A.YEARCODE, A.DIVISIONCODE, A.SYSTEMVOUCHERNO, A.VOUCHERTYPE, A.VOUCHERNO, A.VOUCHERDATE,                                            
            A.CHEQUENO, A.CHEQUEDATE, A.CHEQUEPAIDTO,A.NARRATION, 
            A.ACAMOUNT, A.ACDRCR, A.ACREMARKS, A.ACSERIALNO, 
            A.ACCODE , D.ACHEAD, A.SERIALNO, A.DRCR, A.AMOUNT, A.REMARKS 
     FROM 
     ( 
      SELECT D.ACCODE , D.YEARCODE, D.DIVISIONCODE, D.SYSTEMVOUCHERNO, D.VOUCHERTYPE, D.VOUCHERNO, D.VOUCHERDATE, 
             NVL(D.CHEQUENO, T.PARTYCHEQUENO) CHEQUENO, NVL(D.CHEQUEDATE, T.PARTYCHEQUEDATE) CHEQUEDATE, NVL(D.CHEQUEPAIDTO, T.PARTYCHEQUEDRAWNON) CHEQUEPAIDTO, D.NARRATION,       
             D.AMOUNT , D.DRCR ACDRCR, D.REMARKS ACREMARKS, D.SERIALNO ACSERIALNO,      
             T.ACCODE MAINACCODE, T.SERIALNO, D.DRCR, T.AMOUNT ACAMOUNT, T.REMARKS 
      FROM  
       (    
        SELECT D.ACCODE, D.COMPANYCODE, D.DIVISIONCODE, D.YEARCODE, 
               M.SYSTEMVOUCHERNO, M.VOUCHERTYPE, M.VOUCHERNO, M.VOUCHERDATE, 
        CASE WHEN M.INSTRUCTIONNO IS NULL OR M.INSTRUCTIONNO = '' THEN M.CHEQUENO ELSE M.INSTRUCTIONNO END CHEQUENO, M.CHEQUEDATE, 
               M.CHEQUEDRAWNON CHEQUEPAIDTO, CASE WHEN M.VOUCHERTYPE='PAYMENTS' THEN 'Paid to: ' WHEN M.VOUCHERTYPE='RECEIPTS' THEN 'Received from: ' END || M.PARTY ||  CHR(10) || M.NARRATION NARRATION, 
               ABS(SUM(CASE WHEN D.DRCR = 'D' THEN D.AMOUNT ELSE -D.AMOUNT END)) AMOUNT, 
--               CASE WHEN SIGN(SUM(CASE WHEN D.DRCR  = 'D' THEN D.AMOUNT ELSE -D.AMOUNT END))= -1 THEN 'C' ELSE 'D' END DRCR, 
               CASE WHEN (SUM(CASE WHEN D.DRCR  = 'D' THEN 1 ELSE -1 END)) > 0 THEN 'C' ELSE 'D' END DRCR, 
--               CASE WHEN D.DRCR  = 'D' THEN 'C' ELSE 'D' END DRCR, 
               MAX(D.REMARKS) REMARKS, MIN(D.SERIALNO) SERIALNO  
        FROM ACVOUCHERDETAILS D, ACVOUCHER M 
        WHERE M.COMPANYCODE = '0001' 
          AND M.DIVISIONCODE = '002' 
          AND M.VOUCHERDATE BETWEEN TO_DATE('01/04/2020', 'DD/MM/YYYY') AND TO_DATE('31/03/2021', 'DD/MM/YYYY') 
          AND M.VOUCHERNO NOT LIKE 'OPBAL%' 
          AND M.COMPANYCODE = D.COMPANYCODE 
          AND M.DIVISIONCODE = D.DIVISIONCODE 
          AND M.YEARCODE = D.YEARCODE 
          AND M.SYSTEMVOUCHERNO = D.SYSTEMVOUCHERNO 
        GROUP BY D.ACCODE, D.COMPANYCODE, D.DIVISIONCODE, D.YEARCODE, 
                 M.SYSTEMVOUCHERNO, M.VOUCHERTYPE, M.VOUCHERNO, M.VOUCHERDATE, 
                 M.CHEQUENO , M.CHEQUEDATE, M.PARTY, M.NARRATION,D.PARTYCHEQUEDRAWNON,  M.INSTRUCTIONNO,M.CHEQUEDRAWNON 
       )  D, ACVOUCHERDETAILS T 
      WHERE D.COMPANYCODE = T.COMPANYCODE 
        AND D.DIVISIONCODE = T.DIVISIONCODE 
        AND D.YEARCODE = T.YEARCODE 
        AND D.SYSTEMVOUCHERNO = T.SYSTEMVOUCHERNO 
        AND D.ACCODE <> T.ACCODE  
     ) A, ACACLEDGER L, ACACLEDGER D  
     WHERE A.MAINACCODE = L.ACCODE 
       AND L.COMPANYCODE = '0001' 
       AND A.ACCODE = D.ACCODE 
       AND A.MAINACCODE IN ('S000757') 
       AND D.COMPANYCODE = '0001' 
       AND L.GROUPTYPE IN ('CASH','BANK') 
          AND L.GROUPTYPE IN ('BANK') 
    UNION ALL 
     SELECT 'O' TTYPE, OP.ACCODE OPACCODE, 
             CASE WHEN ABS(SUM(OP.OPENINGDR))>ABS(SUM(OP.OPENINGCR))
             THEN
                 ABS(SUM(OP.OPENINGDR) - SUM(OP.OPENINGCR))
             ELSE
                 0
              END OPENINGDR,
             CASE WHEN ABS(SUM(OP.OPENINGCR))>ABS(SUM(OP.OPENINGDR))
             THEN
                 ABS(SUM(OP.OPENINGCR) - SUM(OP.OPENINGDR))
             ELSE
                 0
              END OPENINGCR,
             CASE WHEN ABS(SUM(OP.OPENINGDR)) >= ABS(SUM(OP.OPENINGCR))
             THEN
                 SUM(OP.OPENINGDR) - SUM(OP.OPENINGCR)
             ELSE
                 SUM(OP.OPENINGCR) - SUM(OP.OPENINGDR)
             END NETOPENING,
            OP.ACCODE AS MAINACCODE, L.ACHEAD AS MAINACHEAD, NULL YEARCODE, NULL DIVISIONCODE, NULL AS SYSTEMVOUCHERNO, NULL AS VOUCHERTYPE, '00000000' AS VOUCHERNO, 
            TO_DATE('01/04/2020','DD/MM/YYYY') AS VOUCHERDATE, 
            NULL AS CHEQUENO, NULL AS CHEQUEDATE,NULL AS CHEQUEPAIDTO, NULL AS NARRATION, 
            0 ACAMOUNT, NULL AS ACDRCR, NULL AS ACREMARKS, 0 ACSERIALNO, 
            NULL AS ACCODE, NULL AS ACHEAD, -1 SERIALNO, NULL AS DRCR, 0 AMOUNT, NULL AS REMARKS 
     FROM 
     ( 
      SELECT ACCODE, 
             CASE WHEN DRCR ='D'THEN  AMOUNT ELSE 0 END  OPENINGDR, CASE WHEN DRCR  ='C' THEN  AMOUNT ELSE 0 END OPENINGCR 
      FROM ACVOUCHERDETAILS 
      WHERE COMPANYCODE='0001' 
        AND DIVISIONCODE='002' 
        AND YEARCODE    = '2020-2021' 
        AND SYSTEMVOUCHERNO LIKE 'OPBAL/%' 
      UNION ALL 
      SELECT ACCODE, 
             CASE WHEN DRCR = 'D' THEN  AMOUNT ELSE 0 END OPENINGDR, CASE WHEN DRCR  = 'C' THEN AMOUNT ELSE 0 END OPENINGCR 
      FROM  ACVOUCHERDETAILS D, ACVOUCHER M 
      WHERE M.COMPANYCODE='0001' 
        AND M.DIVISIONCODE='002' 
        AND M.YEARCODE    = '2020-2021' 
        AND M.VOUCHERDATE < TO_DATE('01/04/2020', 'DD/MM/YYYY') 
        AND M.COMPANYCODE=D.COMPANYCODE 
        AND M.DIVISIONCODE=D.DIVISIONCODE 
        AND M.YEARCODE=D.YEARCODE 
        AND M.SYSTEMVOUCHERNO = D.SYSTEMVOUCHERNO 
        AND D.SYSTEMVOUCHERNO NOT LIKE 'OPBAL/%' 
      ) OP, ACACLEDGER L 
      WHERE OP.ACCODE = L.ACCODE 
       AND L.COMPANYCODE = '0001' 
       AND L.GROUPTYPE IN ('CASH','BANK') 
          AND L.GROUPTYPE IN ('BANK') 
      GROUP BY OP.ACCODE, L.ACHEAD 
  ) A, COMPANYMAST COM, DIVISIONMASTER DIV 
  WHERE NETOPENING + ACAMOUNT <> 0 
    AND COM.COMPANYCODE = '0001' 
    AND COM.COMPANYCODE = DIV.COMPANYCODE 
    AND DIV.DIVISIONCODE='002' 
    AND A.VOUCHERNO='BP/PS/2021/0403/0001'
  ORDER BY VOUCHERDATE, VOUCHERNO, MAINACCODE, SERIALNO, TTYPE 






    
        SELECT D.ACCODE, D.COMPANYCODE, D.DIVISIONCODE, D.YEARCODE, 
               M.SYSTEMVOUCHERNO, M.VOUCHERTYPE, M.VOUCHERNO, M.VOUCHERDATE, 
        CASE WHEN M.INSTRUCTIONNO IS NULL OR M.INSTRUCTIONNO = '' THEN M.CHEQUENO ELSE M.INSTRUCTIONNO END CHEQUENO, M.CHEQUEDATE, 
               M.CHEQUEDRAWNON CHEQUEPAIDTO, CASE WHEN M.VOUCHERTYPE='PAYMENTS' THEN 'Paid to: ' WHEN M.VOUCHERTYPE='RECEIPTS' THEN 'Received from: ' END || M.PARTY ||  CHR(10) || M.NARRATION NARRATION, 
               ABS(SUM(CASE WHEN D.DRCR = 'D' THEN D.AMOUNT ELSE -D.AMOUNT END)) AMOUNT, 
               CASE WHEN SIGN(SUM(CASE WHEN D.DRCR  = 'D' THEN D.AMOUNT ELSE -D.AMOUNT END))= -1 THEN 'C' ELSE 'D' END DRCR, 
               MAX(D.REMARKS) REMARKS, MIN(D.SERIALNO) SERIALNO  
        FROM ACVOUCHERDETAILS D, ACVOUCHER M 
        WHERE M.COMPANYCODE = '0001' 
          AND M.DIVISIONCODE = '002' 
          AND M.VOUCHERDATE BETWEEN TO_DATE('01/04/2020', 'DD/MM/YYYY') AND TO_DATE('31/03/2021', 'DD/MM/YYYY') 
          AND M.VOUCHERNO NOT LIKE 'OPBAL%' 
          AND M.VOUCHERNO='BP/PS/2021/0403/0001'
          AND M.COMPANYCODE = D.COMPANYCODE 
          AND M.DIVISIONCODE = D.DIVISIONCODE 
          AND M.YEARCODE = D.YEARCODE 
          AND M.SYSTEMVOUCHERNO = D.SYSTEMVOUCHERNO 
        GROUP BY D.ACCODE, D.COMPANYCODE, D.DIVISIONCODE, D.YEARCODE, 
                 M.SYSTEMVOUCHERNO, M.VOUCHERTYPE, M.VOUCHERNO, M.VOUCHERDATE, 
                 M.CHEQUENO , M.CHEQUEDATE, M.PARTY, M.NARRATION,D.PARTYCHEQUEDRAWNON,  M.INSTRUCTIONNO,M.CHEQUEDRAWNON 
                 
                 
                 
 
      SELECT D.ACCODE MAINACCODE, D.YEARCODE, D.DIVISIONCODE, D.SYSTEMVOUCHERNO, D.VOUCHERTYPE, D.VOUCHERNO, D.VOUCHERDATE, 
             NVL(D.CHEQUENO, T.PARTYCHEQUENO) CHEQUENO, NVL(D.CHEQUEDATE, T.PARTYCHEQUEDATE) CHEQUEDATE, NVL(D.CHEQUEPAIDTO, T.PARTYCHEQUEDRAWNON) CHEQUEPAIDTO, D.NARRATION,       
             D.AMOUNT ACAMOUNT, D.DRCR ACDRCR, D.REMARKS ACREMARKS, D.SERIALNO ACSERIALNO,      
             T.ACCODE , T.SERIALNO, D.DRCR, T.AMOUNT, T.REMARKS 
      FROM  
       (    
        SELECT D.ACCODE, D.COMPANYCODE, D.DIVISIONCODE, D.YEARCODE, 
               M.SYSTEMVOUCHERNO, M.VOUCHERTYPE, M.VOUCHERNO, M.VOUCHERDATE, 
        CASE WHEN M.INSTRUCTIONNO IS NULL OR M.INSTRUCTIONNO = '' THEN M.CHEQUENO ELSE M.INSTRUCTIONNO END CHEQUENO, M.CHEQUEDATE, 
               M.CHEQUEDRAWNON CHEQUEPAIDTO, CASE WHEN M.VOUCHERTYPE='PAYMENTS' THEN 'Paid to: ' WHEN M.VOUCHERTYPE='RECEIPTS' THEN 'Received from: ' END || M.PARTY ||  CHR(10) || M.NARRATION NARRATION, 
               ABS(SUM(CASE WHEN D.DRCR = 'D' THEN D.AMOUNT ELSE -D.AMOUNT END)) AMOUNT, 
               CASE WHEN SIGN(SUM(CASE WHEN D.DRCR  = 'D' THEN D.AMOUNT ELSE -D.AMOUNT END))= -1 THEN 'C' ELSE 'D' END DRCR, 
               MAX(D.REMARKS) REMARKS, MIN(D.SERIALNO) SERIALNO  
        FROM ACVOUCHERDETAILS D, ACVOUCHER M 
        WHERE M.COMPANYCODE = '0001' 
          AND M.DIVISIONCODE = '002' 
          AND M.VOUCHERDATE BETWEEN TO_DATE('01/04/2020', 'DD/MM/YYYY') AND TO_DATE('31/03/2021', 'DD/MM/YYYY') 
          AND M.VOUCHERNO NOT LIKE 'OPBAL%' 
        AND M.VOUCHERNO='BP/PS/2021/0403/0001'
          AND M.COMPANYCODE = D.COMPANYCODE 
          AND M.DIVISIONCODE = D.DIVISIONCODE 
          AND M.YEARCODE = D.YEARCODE 
          AND M.SYSTEMVOUCHERNO = D.SYSTEMVOUCHERNO 
        GROUP BY D.ACCODE, D.COMPANYCODE, D.DIVISIONCODE, D.YEARCODE, 
                 M.SYSTEMVOUCHERNO, M.VOUCHERTYPE, M.VOUCHERNO, M.VOUCHERDATE, 
                 M.CHEQUENO , M.CHEQUEDATE, M.PARTY, M.NARRATION,D.PARTYCHEQUEDRAWNON,  M.INSTRUCTIONNO,M.CHEQUEDRAWNON 
       )  D, ACVOUCHERDETAILS T 
      WHERE D.COMPANYCODE = T.COMPANYCODE 
        AND D.DIVISIONCODE = T.DIVISIONCODE 
        AND D.YEARCODE = T.YEARCODE 
        AND D.VOUCHERNO='BP/PS/2021/0403/0001'
        AND D.SYSTEMVOUCHERNO='BA0001/002-PVB/2021/00000002'
        AND D.SYSTEMVOUCHERNO = T.SYSTEMVOUCHERNO 
        AND D.ACCODE = T.ACCODE                   
        
        SELECT * FROM ACVOUCHERDETAILS
        WHERE 1=1
        AND SYSTEMVOUCHERNO='BA0001/002-PVB/2021/00000002'

CREATE TABLE GTT_STLDETAILS AS
SELECT TOKENNO, WORKERNAME, 
1.00 PREV_YR_STLBAL_1,1.00 PREV_YR_STLBAL_2, 1.00 CURR_YR_STLBAL1,  1.00 TOTAL_STLBAL,
 1.00  WORKDAYS_CURR_YR, 1.00  STL_AVAILED_YR1, 1.00  STL_AVAILED_YR2,  1.00 STL_AVAILED_YR3, 1.00 TOTAL_STL_AVAILED,
 1.00  STLBAL_DAYS1, 1.00 STLBAL_DAYS2, 1.00 STLBAL_DAYS3, 1.00 TOTAL_STLBAL_DAYS
 FROM WPSWORKERMAST
 
 SELECT * FROM GTT_STLDETAILS
 
 DELETE FROM GTT_STLDETAILS


CREATE TABLE STLBAL_TMP AS
select * from 
GBL_STLBAL
WHERE 1=2


ENTITLE_DAYS, PREV_STLDAYS, STLTAKEN_DAYS, STLBAL_DAYS


select * from (
   select TOKENNO,'ENTITLE_DAYS' CAPTION, ENTITLE_DAYS, YEAR
   from GBL_STLBAL t
)
pivot 
(
   SUM(ENTITLE_DAYS)
   for YEAR in ('2017' AS YR_2017,'2018' AS YR_2018,'2019' AS YR_2019 )
)
order by 1


select * from (
   select TOKENNO,'PREV_STLDAYS' CAPTION, PREV_STLDAYS, YEAR
   from GBL_STLBAL t
)
pivot 
(
   SUM(PREV_STLDAYS)
   for YEAR in ('2017' AS YR_2017,'2018' AS YR_2018,'2019' AS YR_2019 )
)
order by 1

 
select * from (
   select TOKENNO,'STLTAKEN_DAYS' CAPTION, STLTAKEN_DAYS, YEAR
   from GBL_STLBAL t
)
pivot 
(
   SUM(STLTAKEN_DAYS)
   for YEAR in ('2017' AS YR_2017,'2018' AS YR_2018,'2019' AS YR_2019 )
)
order by 1


select * from (
   select TOKENNO,'STLBAL_DAYS' CAPTION, STLBAL_DAYS, YEAR
   from GBL_STLBAL t
)
pivot 
(
   SUM(STLBAL_DAYS)
   for YEAR in ('2017' AS YR_2017,'2018' AS YR_2018,'2019' AS YR_2019 )
)
order by 1






EXEC PROC_RPT_WPSSTLDETAILS('NJ0001','0002','22/01/2020','15/07/2020')


 SELECT * FROM GTT_STLDETAILS
 
 DELETE FROM GTT_STLDETAILS


CREATE TABLE STLBAL_TMP AS
select * from 
GBL_STLBAL
WHERE 1=2

SELECT * FROM WPSWAGESDETAILS	

SELECT TOKENNO, SUM(ATN_DAYS) 
FROM WPSATTENDANCEDAYWISE
WHERE TO_CHAR(FORTNIGHTSTARTDATE,'YYYY')='2019'
GROUP BY TOKENNO

UPDATE GTT_STLDETAILS A SET
WORKDAYS_CURR_YR = 
(
    SELECT SUM(ATN_DAYS) 
    FROM WPSATTENDANCEDAYWISE
    WHERE TO_CHAR(FORTNIGHTSTARTDATE,'YYYY')= '2020'
    AND COMPANYCODE=A.COMPANYCODE
    AND DIVISIONCODE=A.DIVISIONCODE
    AND TOKENNO=A.TOKENNO    
--    GROUP BY TOKENNO
)
WHERE 1=1;

DROP TABLE BIRLANEW.GTT_COMPONENTASSINREPORT CASCADE CONSTRAINTS;

CREATE GLOBAL TEMPORARY TABLE BIRLANEW.GTT_COMPONENTASSINREPORT
(
  WORKERSERIAL        VARCHAR2(10 BYTE),
  TOKENNO             VARCHAR2(10 BYTE),
  EMPLOYEENAME        VARCHAR2(50 BYTE),
  UNITCODE            VARCHAR2(10 BYTE),
  CAT_CD              VARCHAR2(10 BYTE),
  GRD_CD              VARCHAR2(10 BYTE),
  DEPT_CD             VARCHAR2(10 BYTE),
  ESINO               VARCHAR2(20 BYTE),
  PFNO                VARCHAR2(20 BYTE),
  PENSIONNO           VARCHAR2(20 BYTE),
  SEX                 VARCHAR2(10 BYTE),
  EMPLOYEESTATUS      VARCHAR2(20 BYTE),
  DATEOFBIRTH         DATE,
  DATEOFJOIN          DATE,
  DATEOFCONFIRMATION  DATE,
  PFENTITLEDATE       DATE,
  EXTENDEDRETIREDATE  DATE,
  COMPONENTCODE       VARCHAR2(15 BYTE),
  PHASE               NUMBER(4),
  CALCULATIONINDEX    NUMBER(10),
  COMPANYNAME         VARCHAR2(100 BYTE),
  DIVISIONNAME        VARCHAR2(100 BYTE),
  COMPONENTSHORTNAME  VARCHAR2(15 BYTE),
  COMPVALUE           NUMBER,
  PRINTDATE           VARCHAR2(50 BYTE),
  EX1                 NUMBER(10,2),  ------------------------------change varchar2 to number
  EX2                 VARCHAR2(100 BYTE),
  EX3                 VARCHAR2(100 BYTE),
  EX4                 VARCHAR2(100 BYTE),
  EX5                 VARCHAR2(100 BYTE),
  EX6                 VARCHAR2(100 BYTE),
  EX7                 VARCHAR2(100 BYTE),
  EX8                 VARCHAR2(100 BYTE),
  EX9                 VARCHAR2(100 BYTE),
  EX10                VARCHAR2(100 BYTE)
)
ON COMMIT PRESERVE ROWS
NOCACHE;

INSERT INTO GTT_COMPONENTASSINREPORT 

SELECT A.WORKERSERIAL, A.TOKENNO, A.EMPLOYEENAME, A.UNITCODE, A.CATEGORYCODE CAT_CD, A.GRADECODE GRD_CD, A.DEPARTMENTCODE DEPT_CD, 
       A.ESINO, A.PFNO, A.PENSIONNO, A.SEX, A.EMPLOYEESTATUS, A.DATEOFBIRTH, A.DATEOFJOIN, A.DATEOFCONFIRMATION, A.PFENTITLEDATE,  
       A.EXTENDEDRETIREDATE, B.COMPONENTCODE, B.PHASE, B.CALCULATIONINDEX, M.COMPANYNAME, V.DIVISIONNAME, B.COMPONENTSHORTNAME,   
       round(fn_get_compvalue(C.COMPANYCODE,C.DIVISIONCODE,C.YEARMONTH,C.WORKERSERIAL,B.COMPONENTCODE,'PIS COMPONENT REGISTER'),0) COMPVALUE, TO_CHAR(TO_DATE('202004','YYYYMM'),'MON-YYYY') PRINTDATE, 
       NVL(B.PRINTSERIAL,0) EX1, 'Run Date ' || TO_CHAR(SYSDATE,'DD/MM/YYYY  HH:MI:SS AM') EX2,CASE WHEN 'PIS COMPONENT REGISTER'='PIS COMPONENT REGISTER' THEN C.ATTN_SALD ELSE NULL END  EX3, B.COLHEADER EX4, NULL EX5, NULL EX6, NULL EX7, NULL EX8, NULL EX9, NULL EX10 
  FROM PISEMPLOYEEMASTER A,  
       ( SELECT DISTINCT COMPONENTCODE, COMPONENTSHORTNAME, PHASE, CALCULATIONINDEX,PRINTSERIAL,COLHEADER FROM PISCOMPONENTMASTER  
          WHERE COMPANYCODE = 'BJ0056' AND DIVISIONCODE = '0001' 
            AND YEARMONTH = ( 
                             SELECT MAX(YEARMONTH) FROM PISCOMPONENTMASTER  
                              WHERE COMPANYCODE = 'BJ0056' AND DIVISIONCODE = '0001' 
                                AND YEARMONTH<='202004' 
                            ) 
            AND PRINTSERIAL IS NOT NULL 
       ORDER BY PRINTSERIAL) B, 
       ( SELECT * FROM PISPAYTRANSACTION 
          WHERE COMPANYCODE = 'BJ0056' AND DIVISIONCODE = '0001' 
            AND WORKERSERIAL||YEARMONTH IN ( SELECT WORKERSERIAL||MAX(YEARMONTH) 
                                               FROM PISPAYTRANSACTION 
                                              WHERE COMPANYCODE = 'BJ0056' AND DIVISIONCODE = '0001' 
                                                AND YEARMONTH<='202004' 
                                              GROUP BY WORKERSERIAL 
                                           ) 
       ) C, COMPANYMAST M, DIVISIONMASTER V 
WHERE A.COMPANYCODE = C.COMPANYCODE  
  AND A.DIVISIONCODE = C.DIVISIONCODE 
  AND A.WORKERSERIAL = C.WORKERSERIAL  
  AND A.COMPANYCODE=M.COMPANYCODE 
  AND A.COMPANYCODE=V.COMPANYCODE 
  AND A.DIVISIONCODE=V.DIVISIONCODE 
  AND A.COMPANYCODE = 'BJ0056'  
  AND A.DIVISIONCODE = '0001' 
  AND B.COMPONENTCODE IN ('BASIC','DA','ADHOC','PER_ALLOW','SPL_ALLOW','OEPF','OE_NPF','OT_AMT','LEAVE_ENC','CONV_ALOW','MED_ALLOW','HRA','COMPS_ALLOW','MISC_BF') 
 ORDER BY A.TOKENNO, B.PRINTSERIAL
 
 SELECT * FROM GTT_COMPONENTASSINREPORT
 ORDER BY TOKENNO,CALCULATIONINDEX
 
 ORDER BY TOKENNO, TO_NUMBER(EX1)

SELECT A.TOKENNO, B.EMPLOYEENAME,  A.LOANCODE, A.LOANDATE, A.LOANAMOUNT, A.LOAN_BAL, C.INTERESTPERCENTAGE , C.INTERESTAMOUNT 
FROM GBL_LOANBLNC A, PISEMPLOYEEMASTER B, LOANINTEREST C
WHERE A.COMPANYCODE=B.COMPANYCODE
AND A.DIVISIONCODE=B.DIVISIONCODE
AND A.TOKENNO=B.TOKENNO
AND A.COMPANYCODE=C.COMPANYCODE(+)
AND A.DIVISIONCODE=C.DIVISIONCODE(+)
AND A.TOKENNO=C.TOKENNO(+)
AND A.LOANCODE=C.LOANCODE(+)
AND A.LOANDATE=C.LOANDATE(+)

PROC_LOANBLNC 
(
    P_COMPANYCODE  VARCHAR2,
    P_DIVISIONCODE VARCHAR2,
    P_STARTDATE    VARCHAR2,
    P_ENDDATE      VARCHAR2,    
    P_LOANCODE     VARCHAR2,
    P_WORKERSERIAL VARCHAR2 DEFAULT NULL,
    P_MODULE       VARCHAR2 default 'WPS',
    P_WAGEPROCESS  VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'NO', 
    P_TRANTYPE     VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'SALARY'
)

SELECT A.TOKENNO, B.EMPLOYEENAME,  A.LOANCODE, TO_CHAR(A.LOANDATE,'DD/MM/YYYY') LOANDATE, A.LOANAMOUNT, A.LOAN_BAL, NVL(C.INTERESTAMOUNT,0) INTERESTAMOUNT
FROM GBL_LOANBLNC A, PISEMPLOYEEMASTER B, LOANINTEREST C
WHERE A.COMPANYCODE=B.COMPANYCODE
AND A.DIVISIONCODE=B.DIVISIONCODE
AND A.COMPANYCODE=C.COMPANYCODE(+)
AND A.DIVISIONCODE=C.DIVISIONCODE(+)
AND A.TOKENNO=C.TOKENNO(+)
AND A.LOANCODE=C.LOANCODE(+)
AND A.LOANDATE=C.LOANDATE(+)
AND A.TOKENNO=B.TOKENNO
AND A.LOANCODE= 'BL'
AND B.UNITCODE = '01'
AND B.CATEGORYCODE = '10'
AND B.GRADECODE = 'D'

--BIRLA

ALTER TABLE PISCOMPONENTMASTER MODIFY PAYFORMULA VARCHAR2(1000);

--FOR CONVEYANCE ALLOWANCE

CASE WHEN PISMAST.CATEGORYCODE <> '12' THEN
CASE WHEN PISCOMP.CONV_RT >=25000 THEN 4000
WHEN PISCOMP.CONV_RT BETWEEN 17500 AND 24999.99 THEN 3600
WHEN PISCOMP.CONV_RT BETWEEN 12500 AND 17499.99 THEN 3100
WHEN PISCOMP.CONV_RT BETWEEN 7500 AND 12499.99 THEN 2900
WHEN PISCOMP.CONV_RT BETWEEN 6500 AND 7499.99 THEN 2400
WHEN PISCOMP.CONV_RT BETWEEN 5000 AND 6499.99 THEN 1800
WHEN PISCOMP.CONV_RT BETWEEN 3501 AND 5000.99 THEN 1200
WHEN PISCOMP.CONV_RT BETWEEN 1601 AND 3500 THEN 600
ELSE 0 END
ELSE 0
END

 SELECT NVL(B.PARAMETER_VALUE, A.PARAMETER_VALUE) into lv_IntCalcProcName FROM 
    (
        SELECT 1 OPT, 'NA' PARAMETER_VALUE FROM DUAL
    ) A,
    (
        SELECT 1 OPT, PARAMETER_VALUE FROM SYS_PARAMETER
        WHERE PARAMETER_NAME='GENERAL LOAN INTEREST CALCULATION'
        AND PROJECTNAME='PIS' AND ROWNUM=1
    )B
    WHERE A.OPT=B.OPT(+);

    --LOAN INT CALCULATION
    IF lv_IntCalcProcName <> 'NA' THEN
        PRC_GEN_LOAN_INT_CALC(P_COMPCODE,P_DIVCODE,'SWT',NULL,P_END_DT,P_END_DT,P_MODULE,'YES',P_UPDT_TABLENAME);
--        lv_SqlStr := lv_IntCalcProcName||'('''||P_COMPCODE||''','''||P_DIVCODE||''',''SWT'',NULL,'''||P_END_DT||''','''||P_END_DT||''','''||P_MODULE||''',''YES'','''||P_UPDT_TABLENAME||''')';
--        lv_SqlStr := 'BEGIN '||lv_SqlStr||' END';
--        EXECUTE IMMEDIATE lv_SqlStr;
    END IF

 --ADDED FOR INTEREST EMI BALANCE 
IF (C1.INTERESTTYPE = 'R') THEN
                
    lv_ColName := lv_ColName || 'LNBL_'||c1.LOANCODE|| ' = '||nvl(c1.LOAN_BAL,0)||',LIBL_'||c1.LOANCODE||' = '||nvl(c1.LOAN_INT_BAL,0)||',';
    lv_ColName := lv_ColName || 'LINT_'||c1.LOANCODE|| ' = '||nvl(c1.LOAN_INT_BAL,0)||',';
ELSE
 lv_ColName := lv_ColName || 'LNBL_'||c1.LOANCODE|| ' = '||nvl(c1.LOAN_BAL,0)||',LIBL_'||c1.LOANCODE||' = '||nvl(c1.LOAN_INT_BAL,0)||',';
END IF;
                

                    ,INTERESTTYPE, DEDUCTIONTYPE,INTERESTCALCULATIONTYPE
                        
SELECT  NVL(LOAN_INT_BAL,0) LOAN_INT_BAL
FROM GBL_LOANBLNC A, LOANMASTER B
WHERE (NVL(LOAN_BAL,0) + NVL(LOAN_INT_BAL,0))>0
AND A.COMPANYCODE=B.COMPANYCODE
AND A.DIVISIONCODE=B.DIVISIONCODE
AND A.LOANCODE=B.LOANCODE
AND B.INTERESTTYPE='R'
ORDER BY WORKERSERIAL
  
FOR C1 IN (
 SELECT  DISTINCT A.LOANCODE
    FROM GBL_LOANBLNC A, LOANMASTER B
    WHERE (NVL(LOAN_INT_BAL,0))>0
    AND A.COMPANYCODE=B.COMPANYCODE
    AND A.DIVISIONCODE=B.DIVISIONCODE
    AND A.LOANCODE=B.LOANCODE
    AND B.INTERESTTYPE='R'      
)
LOOP                        
                            
lv_SqlStr := lv_SqlStr 
||'UPDATE '||P_UPDT_TABLENAME||' P SET LINT_'||C1.LOANCODE||' =
(
    SELECT  NVL(LOAN_INT_BAL,0) LOAN_INT_BAL
    FROM GBL_LOANBLNC A, LOANMASTER B
    WHERE (NVL(LOAN_BAL,0) + NVL(LOAN_INT_BAL,0))>0
    AND A.COMPANYCODE=B.COMPANYCODE
    AND A.DIVISIONCODE=B.DIVISIONCODE
    AND A.LOANCODE=B.LOANCODE
    AND A.COMPANYCODE=P.COMPANYCODE
    AND A.DIVISIONCODE=P.DIVISIONCODE
    AND A.WORKERSERIAL=P.WORKERSERIAL 
    AND B.INTERESTTYPE=''R''
)          
WHERE 1=1 
AND COMPANYCODE='''||P_COMPCODE||'''
AND DIVISIONCODE='''||P_DIVCODE||'''
AND YEARMONTH='''||lv_YYYYMM||'''';

   
          insert into pIs_error_log(PROC_NAME,ORA_ERROR_MESSG,ERROR_QUERY,PAR_VALUES,FORTNIGHTSTARTDATE, FORTNIGHTENDDATE, REMARKS ) values( lv_ProcName,'',lv_SqlStr,lv_parvalues, lv_fn_stdt, lv_fn_endt, lv_Remarks);
          COMMIT;
          
          execute immediate lv_SqlStr ;
END LOOP;


                            
                
select  WORKERSERIAL,A.LOANCODE,NVL(LOAN_BAL,0) LOAN_BAL, NVL(LOAN_INT_BAL,0) LOAN_INT_BAL
,INTERESTTYPE, DEDUCTIONTYPE,INTERESTCALCULATIONTYPE
                        FROM GBL_LOANBLNC A, LOANMASTER B
                        WHERE (NVL(LOAN_BAL,0) + NVL(LOAN_INT_BAL,0))>0
                        AND A.COMPANYCODE=B.COMPANYCODE
                        AND A.DIVISIONCODE=B.DIVISIONCODE
                        AND A.LOANCODE=B.LOANCODE
                        ORDER BY WORKERSERIAL
                        
                        (SELECT INTERESTTYPE, DEDUCTIONTYPE,INTERESTCALCULATIONTYPE FROM LOANMASTER WHERE LOANCODE=A.LOANCODE) INTERESTTYPE
                        
UPDATE PISPAYTRANSACTION_SWT SET LNBL_PFL=0, LIBL_PFL=0 
 WHERE COMPANYCODE='BJ0056' AND DIVISIONCODE = '0001' 
   AND FORTNIGHTSTARTDATE =  '01-APR-20' AND FORTNIGHTENDDATE = '30-APR-20' 
   AND (NVL(LNBL_PFL,0)+NVL(LIBL_PFL,0))>0 
   AND WORKERSERIAL IN ( SELECT WORKERSERIAL FROM WPSWORKERMAST WHERE COMPANYCODE='BJ0056' AND DIVISIONCODE = '0001' 
                         AND PFSETTELMENTDATE IS NOT NULL )
                         
UPDATE PISPAYTRANSACTION_SWT SET LNBL_STADV = 14880,LIBL_STADV = 0 WHERE COMPANYCODE = 'BJ0056' AND DIVISIONCODE = '0001'  AND YEARMONTH = '202004'  AND WORKERSERIAL = ' 000229'

            (
                SELECT  NVL(LOAN_INT_BAL,0) LOAN_INT_BAL
                FROM GBL_LOANBLNC A, LOANMASTER B
                WHERE (NVL(LOAN_BAL,0) + NVL(LOAN_INT_BAL,0))>0
                AND A.COMPANYCODE=B.COMPANYCODE
                AND A.DIVISIONCODE=B.DIVISIONCODE
                AND A.LOANCODE=B.LOANCODE
                AND A.COMPANYCODE=P.COMPANYCODE
                AND A.DIVISIONCODE=P.DIVISIONCODE
                AND A.WORKERSERIAL=P.WORKERSERIAL 
                AND B.INTERESTTYPE='R'
            )          
            WHERE 1=1 
            AND COMPANYCODE='BJ0056'
            AND DIVISIONCODE='0001'
            AND YEARMONTH='202004'

SELECT * FROM PISCOMPONENTMASTER
WHERE COMPONENTCODE IN ('BASIC','ADHOC','CONV_ALOW','COMPSAVING')

PISMAST

CASE WHEN PISMAST.DATEOFJOIN <= '30-SEP-2019' CASE WHEN PISCOMP.BASIC > 15000 THEN 0 ELSE (CASE WHEN PISCOMP.PF_GROSS > 15000 THEN 15000*0.12 ELSE PISCOMP.PF_GROSS*0.12 END) - (PISCOMP.BASIC*0.12))) END END

CASE WHEN PISTEMPMAST.DATEOFJOIN <= '30-SEP-2019' THEN CASE WHEN PISTEMPCOMP.BASIC > 15000 THEN 0 ELSE ((CASE WHEN PISTEMPCOMP.PF_GROSS > 15000 THEN 15000 ELSE PISTEMPCOMP.PF_GROSS END)*0.12 - (PISTEMPCOMP.BASIC*0.12)) END ELSE 0 END

PISCOMP.BASIC+PISCOMP.DA+PISCOMP.PER_ALLOW+PISCOMP.OEPF


SELECT * FROM PISPAYTRANSACTION


WHERE BASIC < 15000

 CREATE TABLE PIS_SWT_PHASE_DEDN AS 
 
 SELECT PISTEMPATTN.COMPANYCODE, PISTEMPATTN.DIVISIONCODE,PISTEMPATTN.YEARMONTH, PISTEMPATTN.UNITCODE, PISTEMPATTN.CATEGORYCODE, PISTEMPATTN.GRADECODE, PISTEMPATTN.WORKERSERIAL, PISTEMPATTN.TOKENNO, PISTEMPCOMP.ATTN_SALD, PISTEMPCOMP.ATTN_CALCF, 
 PISTEMPCOMP.GROSSEARN, PISTEMPCOMP.TOTEARN 
 , FN_ROUNDOFFRS(NVL(PISTEMPATTN.CAR,0),1,'N') AS CAR, FN_ROUNDOFFRS(NVL(PISTEMPASSIGN.CHOWKIDARI,0),1,'N') AS CHOWKIDARI, 
 FN_ROUNDOFFRS(CASE WHEN PISTEMPMAST.CATEGORYCODE='10' THEN 
 CASE WHEN PISTEMPASSIGN.BASIC < 2000 THEN 5 WHEN PISTEMPASSIGN.BASIC BETWEEN 2000 AND 2999 THEN 8
  WHEN PISTEMPASSIGN.BASIC BETWEEN 3000 AND 7499 THEN 10 ELSE 15 END END,1,'N') AS CLUB, 
  FN_ROUNDOFFRS(CASE WHEN PISTEMPMAST.DATEOFJOIN <= '30-SEP-2019' THEN CASE WHEN PISTEMPCOMP.BASIC > 15000 THEN 0 ELSE ((CASE WHEN PISTEMPCOMP.PF_GROSS > 15000 THEN 15000 ELSE PISTEMPCOMP.PF_GROSS END)*0.12 - (PISTEMPCOMP.BASIC*0.12)) END ELSE 0 END,1,'N') AS COMPSAVING, FN_ROUNDOFFRS(NVL(PISTEMPATTN.DAIRY,0),1,'N') AS DAIRY, FN_ROUNDOFFRS(0,1,'N') AS ELECTRIC, FN_ROUNDOFFRS(CASE WHEN PISTEMPCOMP.ESI_RATE > 21000 THEN  0 ELSE PISTEMPCOMP.ESI_RATE*0.0075  END,1,'H') AS ESI_E, FN_ROUNDOFFRS(NVL(PISTEMPASSIGN.FURNITURE,0),1,'N') AS FURNITURE, FN_ROUNDOFFRS(NVL(PISTEMPATTN.GAMES,0),1,'N') AS GAMES, FN_ROUNDOFFRS(NVL(PISTEMPASSIGN.HR_DEDN,0),1,'N') AS HR_DEDN, FN_ROUNDOFFRS(NVL(PISTEMPASSIGN.ITAX,0),1,'N') AS ITAX, FN_ROUNDOFFRS(NVL(PISTEMPASSIGN.LADIESCLUB,0),1,'S') AS LADIESCLUB, FN_ROUNDOFFRS((PISTEMPCOMP.BASIC+ PISTEMPCOMP.DA)*0.001,1,'S') AS LIBRARY, FN_ROUNDOFFRS(NVL(PISTEMPASSIGN.LIC,0),1,'N') AS LIC,  0  AS LINT_BL,  0  AS LINT_HPF,  0  AS LINT_PFL,  0  AS LINT_SA,  0  AS LINT_STADV,  0  AS LOAN_BL,  0  AS LOAN_HPF,  0  AS LOAN_PFL,  0  AS LOAN_SA,  0  AS LOAN_STADV, FN_ROUNDOFFRS(NVL(PISTEMPATTN.LOTTERY,0),1,'N') AS LOTTERY, FN_ROUNDOFFRS(CASE WHEN SUBSTR(PISTEMPCOMP.YEARMONTH,-2) IN ('06','12') THEN 3 ELSE 0 END,1,'N') AS LWF, FN_ROUNDOFFRS(NVL(PISTEMPATTN.OTHR_DEDN,0),1,'N') AS OTHR_DEDN, FN_ROUNDOFFRS(CASE WHEN PISTEMPMAST.PFAPPLICABLE ='Y' THEN PISTEMPCOMP.PF_GROSS*0.12 ELSE 0 END,1,'S') AS PF_E, FN_ROUNDOFFRS(PISTEMPCOMP.PTAX_GROSS,1,'N') AS PTAX, FN_ROUNDOFFRS(NVL(PISTEMPATTN.RECREATION,0),1,'N') AS RECREATION, FN_ROUNDOFFRS(NVL(PISTEMPATTN.SAL_ADV,0),1,'N') AS SAL_ADV, FN_ROUNDOFFRS(NVL(PISTEMPASSIGN.SCHOOL_BUS,0),1,'N') AS SCHOOL_BUS, FN_ROUNDOFFRS(NVL(PISTEMPATTN.SUBSCRIPTION,0),1,'N') AS SUBSCRIPTION, FN_ROUNDOFFRS((PISTEMPCOMP.PF_GROSS*0.01*PISTEMPASSIGN.VPF_PERC),1,'S') AS VPF 
 FROM PISTEMPMAST, PISTEMPATTN, PISTEMPASSIGN, PISTEMPCOMP, PISTEMPPREV 
 WHERE PISTEMPMAST.WORKERSERIAL = PISTEMPATTN.WORKERSERIAL 
   AND PISTEMPMAST.WORKERSERIAL = PISTEMPASSIGN.WORKERSERIAL 
   AND PISTEMPMAST.WORKERSERIAL = PISTEMPCOMP.WORKERSERIAL 
   AND PISTEMPMAST.WORKERSERIAL = PISTEMPPREV.WORKERSERIAL (+) 
 AND PISTEMPATTN.CATEGORYCODE = '10' 
 AND PISTEMPATTN.GRADECODE = 'D' 
 
SELECT * FROM PIS_ERROR_LOG

DELETE FROM PIS_ERROR_LOG

PISCOMP.BASIC, PISCOMP.ADHOC, PISCOMP.CONV_ALOW,
CASE WHEN (PISCOMP.BASIC+PISCOMP.ADHOC+PISCOMP.CONV_ALOW)>15000
THEN (15000*12/100)-(PISCOMP.BASIC*12/100)
ELSE ((PISCOMP.BASIC+PISCOMP.ADHOC+PISCOMP.CONV_ALOW)*12/100)-(PISCOMP.BASIC*12/100)
END CALC
FROM PISPAYTRANSACTION PISCOMP

SELECT
  REGEXP_SUBSTR('500 Oracle Parkway, Redwood Shores, CA DFD, SA',
                ',[^,]+,') "REGEXPR_SUBSTR"
  FROM DUAL;
  
  
SELECT
  REGEXP_SUBSTR('<<100>><<100>><<100>><<100>>',
                '<<(\d|\w)*>>+/g') "REGEXPR_SUBSTR"
  FROM DUAL;
  

SELECT DISTINCT REGEXP_SUBSTR ('23,34,45,56','[^,]+',1,LEVEL) as "token"
FROM   DUAL
CONNECT BY REGEXP_SUBSTR ('23,34,45,56','[^,]+',1,LEVEL) IS NOT NULL
order by 1

SELECT DISTINCT REGEXP_SUBSTR ('(<<23_11>>+<<34>>)-(<<45>>)*<<56>>','[^<<(w)>>$]+',1,LEVEL) as columnNo
FROM   DUAL
CONNECT BY REGEXP_SUBSTR ('(<<23>>+<<34>>)-<<45>>*<<56>>','[^<<(w)>>]+',1,LEVEL) IS NOT NULL

order by 1


select columnNo from (
SELECT DISTINCT REGEXP_SUBSTR ('<<01_02_04>>+<<01_02_05>>+<<01_02_06>>+<<01_02_07>>','[^<<(w)>>$]+',1,LEVEL) as columnNo
FROM   DUAL
CONNECT BY REGEXP_SUBSTR ('<<01_02_04>>+<<01_02_05>>+<<01_02_06>>+<<01_02_07>>','[^<<(w)>>]+',1,LEVEL) IS NOT NULL
)
where columnNo not in ('*','+','-','/')

select replace(replace('<<01_02_04>>+<<01_02_05>>+<<01_02_06>>+<<01_02_07>>','<<',' '),'>>',' ') from dual

select  01_02_04 + 01_02_05 + 01_02_06 + 01_02_07  from GTTPISITAXCOMPUTATION


SELECT DISTINCT REGEXP_SUBSTR ('(<<01_01_01>>-<<01_01_02>>)*.085','[^<<w>>$]+',1,LEVEL) as columnNo
FROM   DUAL
CONNECT BY REGEXP_SUBSTR ('(<<01_01_01>>-<<01_01_02>>)*.085','[^<<w>>]+',1,LEVEL) IS NOT NULL

SELECT COLUMNNO FROM (
            SELECT DISTINCT REGEXP_SUBSTR ('(<<01_01_01>>-<<01_01_02>>)*.085','[^<<(w)>>$]+',1,LEVEL) AS COLUMNNO
            FROM   DUAL
            CONNECT BY REGEXP_SUBSTR ('(<<01_01_01>>-<<01_01_02>>)*.085','[^<<(w)>>]+',1,LEVEL) IS NOT NULL
        )
        WHERE COLUMNNO NOT LIKE ('%*%') 
        AND COLUMNNO NOT LIKE ('%-%') 
        AND COLUMNNO NOT LIKE ('%+%') 
        AND COLUMNNO NOT LIKE ('%/%')

CREATE TABLE GTT_EXCEL_REPORT
(
  ROWINDEX       NUMBER(20),
  EXCELROWTYPE   VARCHAR2(50 BYTE),
  EXCELROWSTYLE  VARCHAR2(500 BYTE),
  EXCELVALUES    VARCHAR2(3000 BYTE),
  EXCELTAG       VARCHAR2(500 BYTE)
)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------
CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PROC_INSERT_EXCEL_REPORT
(
    P_ROWINDEX NUMBER,
    P_EXCELROWTYPE VARCHAR2,
    P_EXCELROWSTYLE VARCHAR2,
    P_EXCELVALUES VARCHAR2,
    P_EXCELTAG VARCHAR2
)
AS
BEGIN


    INSERT INTO GTT_EXCEL_REPORT(ROWINDEX, EXCELROWTYPE, EXCELROWSTYLE, EXCELVALUES, EXCELTAG)
    VALUES (P_ROWINDEX, P_EXCELROWTYPE, P_EXCELROWSTYLE, P_EXCELVALUES, P_EXCELTAG);
    
END;

FN_GET_ITAX_PERCENTAGE


SELECT  FN_GET_ITAX_PERCENTAGE('0001','0002','2019-2020','00378','600000') TAXAMOUNT FROM DUAL


SELECT SLABFROM, SLABTO,TAXPERCENTAGE,CFFROMLASTSLAB, LASTSLAB, 600000 AMT, CFFROMLASTSLAB + (600000-LASTSLAB)*(TAXPERCENTAGE/100) A
FROM (
    SELECT SLABFROM, SLABTO,TAXPERCENTAGE FROM PISITAXSLAB
    WHERE YEARCODE='2019-2020'
    AND 600000 BETWEEN SLABFROM AND SLABTO
    AND CATEGORY='MALE'
) A,
(
    SELECT MAX(SLABTO) LASTSLAB, MAX(CFFROMLASTSLAB) CFFROMLASTSLAB FROM PISITAXSLAB
    WHERE YEARCODE='2019-2020'
    --AND 300000 BETWEEN SLABFROM AND SLABTO
    AND CATEGORY='MALE'
    AND SLABFROM < 
    (
        SELECT SLABFROM FROM PISITAXSLAB
        WHERE YEARCODE='2019-2020'
        AND 600000 BETWEEN SLABFROM AND SLABTO
        AND CATEGORY='MALE'
    )
)
WHERE 1=1
